# Skyrim:Holds

## Overview

Map showing the different holds

This page lists the nine **holds**, or regions, of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"), each governed by a [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") who lives in the region's capital [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities").

In the absence of a High King, the holds have effectively split from one another, with some even at war with each other. As a consequence, [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") in each hold only care about [crimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") you have committed within that hold, with any bounties you acquire tied to a specific hold. In addition, the [Tribal Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribal_Orcs "Skyrim:Tribal Orcs") faction and [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") track their crime separately from any of the Nord holds.

Many of the holds have distinct climates, such as the Rift being an aspen forest, Falkreath Hold being a pine forest, and Eastmarch being tundra. Snowy mountain environments are also found in most holds.

:   **[Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch")** — A hold in eastern Skyrim, with its capital in Windhelm.
:   **[Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold")** — A hold in southern Skyrim, with its capital in Falkreath.
:   **[Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar")** — A relatively small hold in northwest Skyrim, containing the provincial capital Solitude.
:   **[Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch")** — A hold in northern Skyrim, with its capital in Morthal.
:   **[The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale")** — A hold in northern Skyrim, with its capital in Dawnstar.
:   **[The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach")** — A hold in western Skyrim, with Markarth as its capital.
:   **[The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift")** — A hold in southeast Skyrim, with its capital in Riften.
:   **[Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold")** — A hold in central Skyrim, with its capital in Whiterun.
:   **[Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)")** — A hold in northeast Skyrim, with its capital in the city of Winterhold.

Hollyfrost Farm

**Hollyfrost Farm** is a large farm with a single-roomed farmhouse east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

The farm is owned by [Torsten Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Torsten Cruel-Sea"), but [Tulvur](/wiki/Skyrim:Tulvur "Skyrim:Tulvur"), who lives on the farm, does most of the work. Tulvur and his two dogs, [Tiber](/wiki/Skyrim:Tiber "Skyrim:Tiber") and [Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor_(dog) "Skyrim:Ysgramor (dog)"), live in the spacious L-shaped house on the property. Tulvur has little need of the novice lock that secures the house while he is away since his dogs watch the premises and attack any intruders.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Tulvur](/wiki/Skyrim:Tulvur "Skyrim:Tulvur")  [Tiber](/wiki/Skyrim:Tiber "Skyrim:Tiber")  [Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor_(dog) "Skyrim:Ysgramor (dog)") |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

In the field behind the house are used to cultivate eleven bushels of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and ten [snowberry bushes](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"). At the rear of the property is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). A chicken coop shelters the farm's two [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") while the three [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") wander at will around the farm. There are several [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") as you approach the farm.

| Crops | Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 11 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") | 3 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  10 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") | 1 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  2 [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") | 1 [Chicken's nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Hollyfrost Farm

The interior of Hollyfrost Farm

At the northern end of the farmhouse is a long wooden table with benches either side and a couple of barrels containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") against the north wall. On the table are two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a couple of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). Opposite the entrance on the east wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and on the mantelpiece are three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). To the left of the fireplace is a barrel with a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on top and to the right is a kettle containing four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and a long wooden table and bench. This table holds a couple more potatoes, a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a loaf of bread and a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"). Under the table are two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), while hanging from racks over the table are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") along with two garlic braids, two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the right of the table is a set of shelves holding two bottles of alto wine, three bottles of wine and copies of *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")* and *[Nords Arise!](/wiki/Skyrim:Nords_Arise! "Skyrim:Nords Arise!")*.

Coming out from the south wall is a single unowned bed used by [Tulvur](/wiki/Skyrim:Tulvur "Skyrim:Tulvur"). Further along the south wall is a chair, a food barrel and a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). At the western end of the room is a large double bed coming out from the west wall with an end table on either side, the one to the left has a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") hidden on the floor behind it and a copy of *[Scourge of the Gray Quarter](/wiki/Skyrim:Scourge_of_the_Gray_Quarter "Skyrim:Scourge of the Gray Quarter")* and a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling") on top and the one to the right holds four loose septims. At the foot of the bed is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Along the north wall are a couple more barrels of foodstuffs and a small round table and two chairs with two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top of the table. Finally on the right as you enter, against the west wall is a cupboard and yet another barrel of food. The cupboard only holds clutter, but on top there is a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") and bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat").

## Notes

- In front of this farmhouse is a possible location for the three revelers.

Honeyside

**Honeyside** is a two-story [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") in the northwest corner of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

Kitchen and Bedroom Area

This house, the second-least expensive home that can be obtained, becomes available for purchase during a quest for the [Jarl of Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver"). The quest can be started at the [Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") outside Riften; look for an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") woman, [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta"), working inside the Fishery. However, you need not contact her at the Fishery to start the quest since she can be contacted outside work hours to initiate the quest as well.

Note that the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") will not even mention selling the house until you have completed the associated quests [Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand"), [The Raid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid") and [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand"), and also built a reputation with Riften citizens by doing a few miscellaneous quests for the people of the town (see [I Done Got Thaned!](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!") for details). Honeyside must be purchased from her steward [Anuriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Anuriel "Skyrim:Anuriel") in order to complete the quest and receive the title of [Thane of Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift").

Alternatively, if you give Riften to the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") or conquer it during [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim"), Honeyside can be purchased from [Hemming Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hemming_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Hemming Black-Briar") without having to complete or begin the quests for the Jarl.

Honeyside is a small two-story house, with access from within Riften and from the docks just outside the city. The house comes with a basic kitchen, bedroom, basement with housecarl's quarters, and a dock. A [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"), [Iona](/wiki/Skyrim:Iona "Skyrim:Iona"), will be employed when you have become a Thane of Riften. The garden will regrow after spending 30 in-game days outside of Riften and all its buildings including Honeyside.

2 [Green Apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") - 2 [Mammoth Cheese Bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl") - 5 Potato - 2 [Red Apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") - 5 [Tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") |  | Potions  - 1 leveled [Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison") - 1 leveled [Potion of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength") - 1 leveled [Potion of Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") |  | Recipes  - [Cure Disease Potion Recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease_Potion_Recipe "Skyrim:Cure Disease Potion Recipe") - [Fortify Carry Weight Potion Recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Carry_Weight_Potion_Recipe "Skyrim:Fortify Carry Weight Potion Recipe") - [Invisibility Potion Recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_Potion_Recipe "Skyrim:Invisibility Potion Recipe") - [Restore Health Potion Recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health_Potion_Recipe "Skyrim:Restore Health Potion Recipe") - [Damage Health Poison Recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Damage_Health_Poison_Recipe "Skyrim:Damage Health Poison Recipe") |

## Notes

- Riften does not have a smelter. Since there is no smelter nearby, if you live in Honeyside, you have to travel all the way to [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") to create ingots at the smelter there.
- There are two windows on the outside wall of Honeyside, facing [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse"). However, once you enter, no windows are seen, as the space on the wall where the windows supposedly are located is taken up by the fireplace.
- Any outdoor containers (not inside the building) eventually respawn and delete anything that you may have placed in them. This includes the fish barrel on the deck.
- The music that plays inside the house is environmental music, rather than city music.
- Some of the staged objects obtained when purchasing decorations can't be moved by you (such as forks).
- If Wujeeta dies prior to you completing the quest [Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand") and starting the quest [The Raid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid"), then the only way to purchase the house is if the Imperials occupy Riften.
- This house has a unique back porch entrance that allows you to access the house from outside the city, which can be handy for avoiding guards while you have a price on your head. It's also incredibly helpful if you're encumbered and have a horse. You can hop on your horse, fast travel to the Riften stables, and then ride your [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") right up to the back door for easy loot unloading.
- The three weapon plaques and four weapon racks can all be used to remove quest-marked weapons from your inventory.
- A copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Enchanter's Primer](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Primer "Skyrim:Enchanter's Primer")* can be found on the table in the enchanting laboratory.
- [Adopted](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") children living here will have unique dialogue comments about Riften:

  

  Child's Bedroom

  - *Maramal said I could visit the temple whenever I wanted.* (girls)
  - *Mister [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") gave me an apple, Papa! He seems nice.* (girls)
  - *There are lots of scary people here, Mama. Promise you'll keep me safe?* (girls)
  - *I wanna go swimming, but the guards keep yelling at me. The canal's not that dirty...* (boys)
  - *Mister Brynjolf said he could teach me a lot of neat things when I'm older.* (boys)
- If you ask your spouse "How are the kids?" they will reply with one of the following, depending on their [voicetype](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Dialogue#Adoption_Dialogue "Skyrim:Generic Dialogue"):
  - *Oh fine, love, if you want to bring up little pickpockets. This place is a terrible influence on a child.* (Arrogant)
  - *Just fine, love. The weather here is wonderful, perfect for playing outdoors.* (Neutral)
  - *Well enough. Riften's a tough city, but... it's a tough world. Kid has to learn to stand up for themselves sometime.* (Nord)
  - *Hmph. This city's crawling with thieves. Cowards. Kid could learn some bad habits here.* (Orc)
- Version 4.3.5 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch") prevents the fish barrel on the deck from respawning.

## Bugs

- There are a few bugs which affect all houses, see the [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses#Bugs "Skyrim:Houses") section of the Houses page for details and fixes.
- Jumping onto the bed in the main bedroom while the Housecarl Iona is in the room (but not an active follower) will cause her to say one of her passing phrases, even when you aren't even close to her. Jumping onto anything else doesn't cause this bug, however. **?**
- While the purchase price is officially 8,000 gold, the minimum gold requirement is set to the price for Breezehome, so the jarl's steward will accept as little as 5,000 gold. If you have between 5,000 and 8,000 gold, the steward takes whatever you have.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.13, fixes this bug.
- Visiting the house for the first time before becoming a thane of Riften may prevent you from ever being able to be a thane, and you won't get a housecarl.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Accessing the bookshelves in another home (e.g. [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome")) may cause the bookshelves at Honeyside to appear empty when activated. Any books that were inside the 'empty' shelf may have been deleted.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  - Books can be rescued by removing them individually.
- Switching the enchanting room in Honeyside for a child's bedroom will cause you to lose any equipment stored on the mannequins.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.0.1, addresses this issue. Equipment stored on them will now be transferred to the chest near the double bed upstairs.
  - Switching back to the enchanting Laboratory, all items remain on the mannequins, weapon racks, and plaques and will be recoverable.
- When you buy the garden upgrade, the rest of the options may be removed from the steward's dialogue, making it impossible to buy any other upgrades.
  - To avoid this, purchase the garden last when buying upgrades.
- When you purchase the enchanting area upgrade, the upgrade will not take effect, and the option to purchase it will remain in Anuriel's list of upgrades for purchase.
  -  You can use the following console commands to fix the issue. Note that these commands do not require you to actually buy the enchanting area upgrade. (use the [Hearthfire prefix](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID") for xx)

    ```
    prid xx004258
    disable
    prid c7f1c
    enable
    ```
- The world interactions - Courier Delivering an Important Message or Taunting Adventurer - may spawn inside Honeyside's bedroom. **?**

# Skyrim:Honeystrand Cave

## Overview

Honeystrand Cave

**Honeystrand Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"). It contains only one zone, *[Honeystrand Cave](#Honeystrand_Cave).*

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Honeystrand Cave interior

The cave is northwest of the road intersection south of Ivarstead's southern bridge. A single leveled bear guards the entrance. There are three [beehives](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive "Skyrim:Beehive") nearby (one near the entrance and two on trees in front of the entrance with a vacant beehive between them), making it an ideal place for harvesting [bees](/wiki/Skyrim:Bee "Skyrim:Bee"), [beehive husks](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive_Husk "Skyrim:Beehive Husk"), and [honeycombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeycomb "Skyrim:Honeycomb"). Also near the entrance is a beehive husk, two [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") fungi, a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), and many trees the bears have damaged or killed.

### Honeystrand Cave

The entrance leads directly into a single-chambered cave occupied by up to three bears. Ahead is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") with a growth of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus to the left and a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead)#Bosmer_Male "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") beside it; the bandit carries a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Locked Room](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Locked_Room "Skyrim:The Locked Room")*. Hanging from the roof of the cave and from ledges are three [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") plants, while several [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax") fly around the rear of the cave. Next to the west wall is a dead [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") with another patch of imp stool, and against the north wall is a patch of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungus. The floor of the cave is littered with old bones, both human and animal, including a lootable skeleton.

## Notes

- A dead woodcutter's campsite is northeast of the cave, up a hill toward [Geirmund's Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Geirmund's Hall"). Southeast of the campsite on the highest peak is a strange [chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") nest built on barrels and skeletal remains guarded by a novice [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"). Three of the chickens suddenly die as you approach. The fourth chicken, already dead, may be revived by the necromancer to attack. Near the nest in an open box are three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and one [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"). A [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") plant is also nearby.
- Honeystrand Cave appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as [Honeystrand Hill](/wiki/Online:Honeystrand_Hill "Online:Honeystrand Hill").

Honningbrew Meadery

**Honningbrew Meadery** is a small [meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") owned by [Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn "Skyrim:Sabjorn").

Honningbrew Meadery before completion of Dampened Spirits

Honningbrew Meadery after completion of Dampened Spirits

It produces [Honningbrew Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") in competition with [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). The site contains two buildings: *[Honningbrew Meadery](#Honningbrew_Meadery)* and *[Honningbrew Boilery](#Honningbrew_Boilery)*, both of which share a *[basement](#Honningbrew_Basement)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Eimar](/wiki/Skyrim:Eimar "Skyrim:Eimar")  [Mallus Maccius](/wiki/Skyrim:Mallus_Maccius "Skyrim:Mallus Maccius") [Fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Fence") \*  [Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn "Skyrim:Sabjorn") (Owner) [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink") † |

\* This person only becomes a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)") and is placed in charge of the meadery after completing the quest [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits").
† This person is no longer available after completing the quest Dampened Spirits.

### Thieves Guild

- **[Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits")**: Put [Maven Black-Briar's](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") competition out of business.
- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

### Exterior

The meadery is at the crossroad by the bridges southeast of Whiterun. There are two "Honningbrew Meadery" signs, one on either side of the path leading to the entrance to the meadery, which is always unlocked. There is a third sign to the right of the entrance to the boilery, which is kept locked and requires a key. Stacked around the entrance to the boilery are many barrels, some containing bottles of Honningbrew Mead, and others regular [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). There are numerous flowers and plants in the immediate vicinity, as well as [monarch butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Monarch_Butterfly "Skyrim:Monarch Butterfly") and [blue butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly") during the day and [luna moths](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth "Skyrim:Luna Moth") and [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") in the evenings and at night.

| Plants | Animals |
| --- | --- |
| 2 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  3 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender")  1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  4 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  1 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch")  1 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") | 1 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") |

### Honningbrew Meadery

Storage area

The meadery is the larger right-hand building. A counter is in front of the wall opposite the entrance. Prior to starting the quest [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits"), Sabjorn and his employees, [Eimar](/wiki/Skyrim:Eimar "Skyrim:Eimar") and [Mallus Maccius](/wiki/Skyrim:Mallus_Maccius "Skyrim:Mallus Maccius"), can be found here. Sabjorn is happy to buy and sell foodstuffs. On your immediate left upon entering is a bookcase holding eight common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), and on your right is an end table with a bowl of [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") on top. The counter has five bottles of Honningbrew Mead, a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), and a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") on top, and a further twenty-one bottles of mead underneath. Behind the bar are two sets of shelves holding nine more bottles of mead and another sweet roll, as well as some cheap crockery. Against the east wall is a long wooden table with several mead barrels on top, with a bowl containing four honey nut treats beside them. In both the northeastern and northwestern corners are small tables and chairs, holding a total of four bottles of Honningbrew Mead, an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), two red apples, a honey nut treat, and a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"). A third small table is against the east wall, with a single bottle of Honningbrew Mead and a sweet roll on top. In the southwestern corner is a stack of barrels containing more bottles of Honningbrew Mead. There are double doors in the middle of the west wall leading to the storage area.

After starting the quest Dampened Spirits, when you enter you will find Sabjorn standing in front of the counter alone with two dead [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") on the floor, one at either end of the room. After speaking with Sabjorn and convincing him to let you help, he will hand you a copy of the [Honningbrew Meadery key](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery_Key "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery Key"), which opens both the door into the basement and also the door to his sleeping quarters in the loft.

The storage area is filled with many stacks of barrels containing bottles of Honningbrew Mead and sacks of foodstuffs. Towards the rear of the room is a set of shelves holding eighteen bottles, a narrow table with five more bottles on top, and a bucket underneath containing four more bottles. At the southern end of the room is a flight of stairs leading down to a door to *[Honningbrew Basement](#Honningbrew_Basement)*, which is locked and requires the Honningbrew Meadery key given by Sabjorn. There are three [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") at the top of the stairs, and another at the bottom by the door.

At the northern end of the room are four more bottles of Honningbrew Mead on top of barrels. In the northeastern corner is a doorway to a flight of stairs leading up to the loft. Under the stairs is one more bottle of mead. The loft is only partially boarded along the west, south, and part of the east walls, with a railing overlooking the storage area below. Against the west wall is a single owned bed, with a wall shelf above it holding a copy of *[The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v2 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2")*, a red apple, and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). Against the south wall is a small square table, with a bottle of Honningbrew Mead on top and an owned bedroll beside it. At the end of the boarding on the east wall is an adept-locked door, which is opened using the Honningbrew Meadery key given by Sabjorn.

You will need to visit Sabjorn's quarters to access the information needed for [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") for the quest Dampened Spirits. His bedroom contains a large owned double bed coming out from the north wall, with end tables on either side. On top of the end table on the left is a bottle of Honningbrew Mead, a red apple, and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), while on the end table on the right is a common book. Under the bed is a bowl containing a bottle of Black-Briar Mead. Against the east wall is an expert-locked door; to the left is Sabjorn's dresser, which is locked and requires a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn%27s_Dresser_Key "Skyrim:Sabjorn's Dresser Key"). It has a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and a bowl containing [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat") on top. To the right of the door is a tall wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). Against the south wall is a long wooden table, with a plate of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") and two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a note entitled *[Have Need of Cynric](/wiki/Skyrim:Have_Need_of_Cynric_(Sabjorn) "Skyrim:Have Need of Cynric (Sabjorn)")* from Maven, and an empty display case. To the right is a small cupboard. The west wall has a set of shelves against it holding ten common books, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a bottle of wine. To the left on the floor is a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), and to the right is a small wooden table and two chairs. On the table is a bottle of alto wine, two honey nut treats, a common book, and a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Game at Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Game_at_Dinner "Skyrim:A Game at Dinner")*.

The expert-locked door leads to a small room with two wall shelves behind the door on the north wall. On these is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and some fine crockery, and next to them is a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes. Opposite, against the south wall is a long end table with three [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), a medium coin purse, a [silver necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace"), an empty [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), and the [Honningbrew Decanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Decanter "Skyrim:Honningbrew Decanter"), a unique item prized by [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") as part of the quest [The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny"). To the right of the end table, on the floor, is a large coin purse.

### Honningbrew Basement

Honningbrew Basement

The basement only becomes accessible once you start the quest Dampened Spirits and receive the Honningbrew Meadery key from Sabjorn. Upon entering, you will see several dead skeevers and a bear trap in front of you. Off to the left is a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Venomfang_Skeever "Skyrim:Venomfang Skeever") that has been magically enhanced to be poisonous, similarly to [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). The room contains several large vats and large stacks of unusable barrels. In the middle of the east wall is a set of shelves holding five bottles of Honningbrew Mead, and on the south wall, at the far end, are two barrels containing more bottles of Honningbrew Mead with a set of shelves that have been knocked over to reveal a tunnel behind. Two bear traps have been set in front of the hole.

Just inside the tunnel is another dead skeever, near where the tunnel descends to the south. At the bottom, the tunnel turns to the east, then opens into a cave containing four more skeevers, some of which are venomous. The cave has quite a lot of vegetation that can obscure your view. On the ground are three bottles of Honningbrew Mead, and against the east wall a barrel containing more bottles of mead. To the north is a narrow tunnel leading onwards. Follow the tunnel as it continues to descend past a web sac containing a [skeever tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail") near a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") on the wall and takes three turns. Just after the final turn to the east, the tunnel opens into another cave, with several frostbite spiders, more web sacs, and many glowing mushrooms on the walls. Again to the north is a narrow tunnel, which after two turns opens into a cave containing only several unusable barrels, an unusable crate, and two bear traps. At the far end, a tunnel with a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") across the entrance that triggers a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap descends to the east. Keep following the tunnel as it takes two turns before opening into another cave. You will be immediately spotted by a skeever, unless your [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill is exceptional. Also in the cave are several other skeevers, some venomous, and a mad alchemist named [Hamelyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamelyn "Skyrim:Hamelyn").

Once they are all defeated, loot Hamelyn to find [his journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamelyn%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hamelyn's Journal"), which explains how he was exiled from the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") and jailed in Whiterun for being a danger and insane; he escaped the jail, and plotted his revenge against both the people of Whiterun and Winterhold. To the southeast you will find the skeever nest to the right of an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). Between the nest and the lab is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), two leveled [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and a copy of the Sneak skill book *[Three Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Three_Thieves "Skyrim:Three Thieves")*. To the north is another narrow tunnel that takes two turns as it rises and eventually leads to the basement under the boilery. At the exit from the tunnel are two more bear traps and another set of shelves that has been moved to reveal the tunnel. The basement contains many large vats and barrels, but only one, on your left as you enter the basement, contains bottles of Honningbrew Mead. At the far end, on the north wall, is a door leading up into the boilery itself.

### Honningbrew Boilery

Honningbrew Boilery interior

Honningbrew Boilery exterior

The boilery contains four large boilers, three of which have fires under them. They are on a raised section in the middle of the room. To the right of the vat without the fire is a long wooden table with a bowl containing three bottles of Honningbrew Mead, two more separate bottles of mead, and a sweet roll. To the right of the table is a barrel containing more bottles of mead. Around the outside of the room are several crates, food sacks, barrels containing more bottles of mead, and a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes. In the middle of the north wall is a door leading outside, which is locked and requires the [Honningbrew Brewhouse key](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Brewhouse_Key "Skyrim:Honningbrew Brewhouse Key") on the hook to the right of the door. To the left of the door is a flight of wooden stairs leading up to a balcony that runs around the edge of three of the walls to provide access to the lids of the boilers. At the top of the stairs is a small cupboard, and on the balcony are several food sacks and a few barrels containing more bottles of mead. In the middle of the east wall is an apprentice-locked chest containing minor loot. At the far end of the balcony is a dresser containing clothes.

Once you have added the poison to the boiler, the quest objective will instruct you to return to Sabjorn. When you reenter the meadery, you will find the commander of the guard in Whiterun, [Commander Caius](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Caius "Skyrim:Commander Caius"), with Sabjorn standing behind the counter, and Mallus Maccius standing at the other end of the room. The skeevers and blood have been cleaned up, and Sabjorn has been delaying the commander awaiting the all-clear from you. Sabjorn will tell you that you'll have to wait until the end of the tasting for your pay. Once Sabjorn has been taken to [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") by the commander, you will be free to speak to Mallus, who, after a short monologue, will hand you the key to Sabjorn's dresser. The dresser contains a [promissory note](/wiki/Skyrim:Promissory_Note "Skyrim:Promissory Note") and a few [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Once you have returned to Maven, Mallus will be available as a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)").

## Notes

- The main building will respawn after ten days. However, *Honningbrew Basement* and *Honningbrew Boilery* never respawn.
- Before the completion of the quest Dampened Spirits, there is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the left of the entrance door, placed there because of the gold, silver necklace, silver ingots, and Honningbrew Decanter behind an expert-locked door inside.
- Upon the completion of the quest Dampened Spirits, a  "Fence") Fence shadowmark replaces the  "Loot") Loot shadowmark, with Mallus Maccius as the fence, and "Black-Briar Meadery" signs replace the "Honningbrew Meadery" signs.
- Despite Mallus suggesting it as an alternate point of entry, you cannot enter the brewhouse until after you make your way through the tunnels for the first time. The front door is unpickable and can only be unlocked using the key that you find inside the boilery.
- During [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun"), the building will be apprentice-locked. If you pick the lock, Sabjorn will be back in charge with both him and Mallus Maccius telling you to get out and treating you as if they don't know you. You will be unable to trade with either of them.
- One [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay_Deposit "Skyrim:Clay Deposit")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is beside the stone bridge on the river bank just northeast of the meadery.
- *Honning* is the Danish and Norwegian word for *honey*.

## Bugs

- After you finish Dampened Spirits, the Honningbrew Mead barrels outside of the meadery may not be changed to Black-Briar Mead barrels.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. Proper enable parents have been added to the existing barrels as well as the created replacement barrels. The barrels were also missing their ownership settings.
- Two barrels in the basement of the building, right before the entrance to the cave, can be seen merged together in the same location with identical X, Y, and Z positions, but with different form ID's (000A6433 and 000A6434).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. Both aforementioned barrels are now separate from each other.

# Skyrim:Honor Thy Family

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [RIM](/wiki/User:RIM "User:RIM"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Regain the trust of your fellow Assassins.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | Readmission into the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") |
| ID: | DBEviction |

*"You disrespected the Brotherhood. And it'll cost you."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").
2. Pay Nazir a fine.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest is received after attacking a member of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), accidentally or not. Pay a fine to Nazir to get back in the good graces of the family, which completes this quest. You cannot accept or complete any contracts until you pay the fine and Dark Brotherhood members will refuse to talk to you while suspended from the guild.

The fine will be 500 gold if you are a regular member, but if you have completed [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"), the amount will be reduced to 300 gold.

## Notes

- The [Spectral Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Spectral_Assassin "Skyrim:Spectral Assassin") is considered a member of the Dark Brotherhood, so if you attack him to the point that he turns hostile then you will have to pay a fine.

- Even if you are not a member of the Dark Brotherhood, this quest can still be triggered while completing the quest [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") if you calm any of the assassins and talk to them before you kill them. If calmed, Nazir can still be paid the 500 gold, after which he will repeatedly tell you to go back and speak with Astrid (even though the quest can only begin if she is already dead).

## Bugs

- All contract victims are placed in the Dark Brotherhood faction at some point, and feeding on them as a vampire, or their corpse as a cannibal (with the [Ring of Namira](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Namira "Skyrim:Ring of Namira")) may trigger this quest, though it won't actually begin until the next time you talk to a Dark Brotherhood member.
- Sometimes this quest might be triggered after you have fully upgraded the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary").
- Sometimes this quest might be triggered even after completing [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") if you use one of the Dark Brotherhood characters as a [Dead Thrall.](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall") Needless to say, it cannot be completed.
- Causing damage to the assassin's corpse in [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End") using the spell [Unbounded Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbounded_Storms "Skyrim:Unbounded Storms") seems to have triggered this quest. **?**
- Once the fine has been paid, it is possible to trigger the fine dialogue again if you speak to Nazir too quickly.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBEviction stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBEviction`.

# Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Honorhall Orphanage ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Honorhall+Orphanage)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| RiftenHonorhallOrphanage | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Honorhall Orphanage

**Honorhall Orphanage** is located in the southern part of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). It consists of one zone, *[Honorhall Orphanage](#Honorhall_Orphanage)*.

It houses four orphans and is run by the generally despised headmistress, [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind") (an apparently self-given nickname). Grelod's meek assistant, [Constance Michel](/wiki/Skyrim:Constance_Michel "Skyrim:Constance Michel"), lives in the orphanage as well. A fifth orphan, [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino"), whom you encounter in the quest [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost"), lived there temporarily until running away.

Installation of the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on allows you to [adopt](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") orphans from Honorhall Orphanage.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind") (Caretaker)  [Constance Michel](/wiki/Skyrim:Constance_Michel "Skyrim:Constance Michel") (Assistant)  [Francois Beaufort](/wiki/Skyrim:Francois_Beaufort "Skyrim:Francois Beaufort")  [Hroar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroar "Skyrim:Hroar")  [Runa Fair-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Runa_Fair-Shield "Skyrim:Runa Fair-Shield")  [Samuel](/wiki/Skyrim:Samuel "Skyrim:Samuel") |

With Hearthfire installed, the death of the parents of a child will cause the child to be relocated to the orphanage.

## Related Quests

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

## Honorhall Orphanage

The main bedroom for the children

Grelod's bedroom

The entrance is to the west of [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep"). You enter into a reception room with two benches on your right and a dresser in front of you, with the door into the dining room to the left. On the dresser there is [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). There are two barrels to the left of the entrance. In the dining room there are two long tables with benches either side holding a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), two raw [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and a food barrel in the northwest corner of the room. There are two doors to the west and a doorway to the south of this room.

The doorway leads into the main bedroom for the children, and contains five beds, three chests, and a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front. There is a door to an enclosed outside area to the east and two double doors in to the south. The one on the left is Grelod's bedroom and contains a double bed, a wardrobe, two end tables, a dresser, and a table and chair. On the end tables is a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a bottle of wine, a sample of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a copy of *[The Woodcutter's Wife](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Woodcutter%27s_Wife "Skyrim:The Woodcutter's Wife")*, and a copy of *[The Bear of Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bear_of_Markarth "Skyrim:The Bear of Markarth")*. On the dresser is a bottle of Nord mead, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and a copy of *[The Cabin in the Woods](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cabin_in_the_Woods "Skyrim:The Cabin in the Woods")*, with a pair of boots beside it. On the table there is a bottle of wine, a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), a wooden plate containing a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and two [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse")—one medium, one large. The second double door leads to the punishment room, a small room containing three sets of shackles.

The two doors off of the dining room lead to Constance Michel's bedroom and a storeroom respectively. Constance's bedroom contains a dresser, end table, and a single bed. There is a wooden bowl containing a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") mountain flower on the dresser, a bottle of alto wine on the end table, and a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Purloined Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Purloined_Shadows "Skyrim:Purloined Shadows")* on the floor between the end table and bed.

The storeroom contains a cupboard with a bowl of bonemeal on top, a large shelving unit holding five potatoes, two loaves of bread, a cabbage, three [eidar cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") and two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), various sacks on the floor, a barrel and a small table, with a basket of potatoes between these. On the table are four potatoes, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a loaf of bread, and bottles of alto wine and Nord mead. There are three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), three [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), four [dried elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), and three [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") samples hanging from the ceiling.

## Notes

- The punishment room is mentioned in [Runa Fair-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Runa_Fair-Shield "Skyrim:Runa Fair-Shield")'s dialogue: *"I hate her. Everyone hates her. She's the meanest person I ever met. Sometimes she even locks us in the... room."*
- If more children become orphans after Grelod's death, her room will be transformed to contain six beds which the new orphans sleep in randomly.

## Bugs

- Based on his dialogue, Aventus Aretino is supposed to return to the orphanage after the completion of the Innocence Lost quest. However, he remains alone in his Windhelm home long thereafter.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, fixes this bug.
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3 created another bug. Although Aventus now returns to Honorhall Orphanage after completion of Innocence Lost with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3, he doesn't sleep here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Orphans transferred to Riften are not assigned an ownership faction and thus cannot use various markers in the orphanage.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.5, fixes this bug.
- None of the beds here are owned by the children.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Horgeir's House

## Overview

Horgeir's House

**Horgeir's House** is a residence in the northwestern part of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), located next to [Lylvieve Family's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family%27s_House "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family's House") and across from [Four Shields Tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Shields_Tavern "Skyrim:Four Shields Tavern").

It is the home of [Horgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir "Skyrim:Horgeir"), his wife [Olda](/wiki/Skyrim:Olda "Skyrim:Olda"), and his brother [Lodvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Lodvar "Skyrim:Lodvar"). It consists of one zone, *[Horgeir's House](#Horgeir.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Horgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir "Skyrim:Horgeir")  [Lodvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Lodvar "Skyrim:Lodvar")  [Olda](/wiki/Skyrim:Olda "Skyrim:Olda") |

## Exterior

| Plants |
| --- |
| 1 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  1 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") |

## Horgeir's House

Fireplace and single bed area

The front door to this small home opens to a view of the fireplace at the center, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") at its base and an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") on the mantel. On the floor to the right of the fireplace is a woven basket containing four [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and five [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), while four pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") sit in a pile to the left.

On the east side of the home is a small bedroom area, with a single bed in the northeast corner. A [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") can be found propped against the wall next to the head and two [drums](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") sit at the foot of the bed. Beneath the bed is a copy of the book *[Spirit of Nirn](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_Nirn "Skyrim:Spirit of Nirn")*. In the southeast corner, a small table holds a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"). On the opposite side of the home, another bedroom area can be found in the northwest corner, with a double bed along the north wall. Next to the bed, a small table holding two bottles of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") sits in the corner. A non-respawning wardrobe is situated next to the table, with a small non-respawning chest to its left.

Dining area and double bed area

The south wall on the west side of the home is host to a cozy dining area. A respawning food barrel rests next to the front door with some [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") on top, next to a large dining table with a pleasant array of food: an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), one [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a serving of [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a sweet roll, an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a serving of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), and two bottles of Nord mead. To the right of the table sits a woven basket containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), with a hanging rack above it holding three freshly caught [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). A set of shelves next to the basket holds an additional two leeks, a garlic bulb, and three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), along with an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), some [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on top. Above the shelves are several hanging ingredients, including two garlic braids, three portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and one dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). A respawning meat barrel and respawning food barrel sit in the corner next to the shelves.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Horgeir's House Key") to which is carried by Horgeir, Lodvar, and Olda.

# Skyrim:Horker Island

## Overview

Horker Island

**Horker Island** is a large island east of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") occupied by [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker").

## Related Quests

- **[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(quest) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (quest)")**: Find the treasure of [Haknir Death-Brand](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand").
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

The entrance to [Gyldenhul Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Gyldenhul_Barrow "Skyrim:Gyldenhul Barrow") is on the northwest shore, while the horkers are mainly found on the eastern and northern shores. There are numerous [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Ashen Grass Pod") plants found on the island, and an [ebony ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Ebony Ore Vein") on the eastern shore against a large rock. For an easy approach, either the southern or northwestern beaches offer the shortest distance over water. The island has a rocky spine limiting access from north to south or east to west. There are several [Felsaad terns](/wiki/Skyrim:Felsaad_Tern "Skyrim:Felsaad Tern") flying over the island at any time, no matter the weather.

The beach to the south has an overturned rowboat with several barrels around it, two of which are fish barrels. [Saden's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saden%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Saden's Journal") lies on top of a crate. Traveling counter-clockwise around the island to the eastern shore, there are several horkers including a named horker, [Lord Tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Tusk "Skyrim:Lord Tusk"), a total of four dead [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") along the beach, the gory remains of more humans amid blood splatters, and the broken remains of a larger boat, with the front half wedged up on the rocks at the shoreline and other half under the water. Just below the visible portion of the boat underwater is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") beside an expert-locked [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") and a [clam](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam"). There are three [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") clusters and a patch of [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") on the other half of the boat, either on the deck or the hull.

Heading inland due west from the boat will lead you to the corpse of [Saden](/wiki/Skyrim:Saden "Skyrim:Saden") and a unique [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), [Horksbane](/wiki/Skyrim:Horksbane "Skyrim:Horksbane"), which as the name suggests does increased damage to horkers. Continuing up the rise from the corpse will bring you to an area covered in human skulls and bones, with an unlocked chest, a random enchanted [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), and a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"). Farther along the shore to the north is the mast of another sunken ship sticking out of the water. There is another Nordic barnacle cluster on the hull below the mast, while farther north on the beach is a master-locked wooden chest.

Continuing northwest along the isle's edge past a short section without a beach, with only rocks disappearing into the water, you will reach the western shore. There is a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") against the rocks near two rowboats pulled up onshore. Behind several tall rocks standing upright along the shore is the entrance to Gyldenhul Barrow. A [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush grows just to the left of the master-locked entrance, which is guarded by two leveled reavers. Once you have found and emptied all four chests during the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(quest) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (quest)"), you will receive a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Gyldenhul_Barrow_Key "Skyrim:Gyldenhul Barrow Key") that will open this door.

## Notes

- Notably, Saden's Journal is the only book in the game with a value of 1 gold. The only book worth less is the [Imperial Missive](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Missive_(Battle-Born) "Skyrim:Imperial Missive (Battle-Born)") found in the [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born").
- Lord Tusk respawns every time the island resets.

# Skyrim:Horse Whisperer

## Overview

Locate and tame wild horses

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to a [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").
2. Purchase a map and book for 250 gold.
3. *(Optional)* Track down and [tame](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") all seven wild horses.

### Horse Tamer

Upon reading *[Soran's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Soran%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Soran's Journal")* located on [Urag gro-Shub's](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") desk in [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"), this quest will automatically begin and will direct you to the nearest [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").[*verification needed — how is this selected?*] You will need to speak with the hostler, i.e. the NPC who sells [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). (NOTE: I received the opportunity at the Whiterun Stables in a new game to buy the map without performing any of the actions previously outlined.) You will be presented with the option to purchase a wild horse map for 250 gold. You will receive both a [Map of Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Map of Wild Horses") and a book called *[Wild Horse Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse_Notes "Skyrim:Wild Horse Notes")*. In conjunction with reading the book, the map can be examined in your inventory in order to locate seven [wild horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse "Skyrim:Wild Horse").

Upon making this purchase, this quest will conclude. However, you will then receive seven miscellaneous objectives tasking you with locating and [taming](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") every wild horse. The objectives themselves are rather useless as they do not provide a map marker for the individual horses. Instead, you will need to use the map and book to travel to the approximate location and search for the horse. The book itself advises that [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") will be useful in carrying out this task. Note that wild horses will flee if you get too close, so it may help to sneak up on them.

To tame a wild horse, you must remain mounted on the horse while it bucks. It has a chance to ragdoll you when bucking, which will force you to chase down the fleeing horse once you get back on your feet. [Sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") can help prevent the horse from fleeing too far. Once mounted for a sufficient length of time, the horse becomes an owned mount. If you switch to a different mount, it will slowly make its way back to the location you originally found it.

### Find and tame the Black Horse

This horse can be found northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), just south of the map marker for [Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove"). The book refers to nearby ruins, the ruins in question being Cracked Tusk Keep. This location is close to a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer")'s ritual site, and the resident necromancer might interrupt the taming process if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Chestnut Horse

This horse can be found east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), along the path leading towards [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp"). It's off of the north side of the road, just under halfway from Helgen to the Falkreath Stormcloak Camp.

### Find and tame the Dapple Brown Horse

This horse can be found in the forest south of [Solitude Sawmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill"), across the river but before you reach the [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mound "Skyrim:Dragon Mound"). This can obviously be a dangerous place to tame a horse if the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") is still nearby.

### Find and tame the Grey Spotted Horse

This horse can be found up the hill to the north of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm"). Beware the nearby [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") who will attack you and the horse if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Pale Mare

This horse can be found among a group of snowy pines just south of [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow").

### Find and tame the Red Horse

This horse can be found on the plains of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), northwest of [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"). It is a very easy mount to locate and tame, particularly at the start of the game.

### Find and tame the White Spotted Horse

This horse can be found directly west of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), west of the road, on a green cliff overlooking the volcanic tundra below.

## Notes

- Each wild horse can be [named](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Horse_NamingCC "Skyrim:Horses") and [saddled](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#SaddlesCC "Skyrim:Horses"), which are two other mechanics added by this Creation. To do this, you must visit a stable with the horse as your active mount.
- Horses on even slight inclines will sometimes throw you further than expected, possibly causing significant damage or killing you.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted`.

# Skyrim:Horse Whisperer

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. | Location(s): | [The Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") |

| ID: | ccBGSSSE034\_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse01\_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse02\_Black, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse03\_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse04\_Pale, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse05\_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse06\_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse07\_BrownSpotted |
| Added by: | [Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses") |

Locate and tame wild horses

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to a [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").
2. Purchase a map and book for 250 gold.
3. *(Optional)* Track down and [tame](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") all seven wild horses.

### Horse Tamer

Upon reading *[Soran's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Soran%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Soran's Journal")* located on [Urag gro-Shub's](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") desk in [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"), this quest will automatically begin and will direct you to the nearest [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").[*verification needed — how is this selected?*] You will need to speak with the hostler, i.e. the NPC who sells [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). (NOTE: I received the opportunity at the Whiterun Stables in a new game to buy the map without performing any of the actions previously outlined.) You will be presented with the option to purchase a wild horse map for 250 gold. You will receive both a [Map of Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Map of Wild Horses") and a book called *[Wild Horse Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse_Notes "Skyrim:Wild Horse Notes")*. In conjunction with reading the book, the map can be examined in your inventory in order to locate seven [wild horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse "Skyrim:Wild Horse").

Upon making this purchase, this quest will conclude. However, you will then receive seven miscellaneous objectives tasking you with locating and [taming](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") every wild horse. The objectives themselves are rather useless as they do not provide a map marker for the individual horses. Instead, you will need to use the map and book to travel to the approximate location and search for the horse. The book itself advises that [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") will be useful in carrying out this task. Note that wild horses will flee if you get too close, so it may help to sneak up on them.

To tame a wild horse, you must remain mounted on the horse while it bucks. It has a chance to ragdoll you when bucking, which will force you to chase down the fleeing horse once you get back on your feet. [Sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") can help prevent the horse from fleeing too far. Once mounted for a sufficient length of time, the horse becomes an owned mount. If you switch to a different mount, it will slowly make its way back to the location you originally found it.

### Find and tame the Black Horse

This horse can be found northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), just south of the map marker for [Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove"). The book refers to nearby ruins, the ruins in question being Cracked Tusk Keep. This location is close to a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer")'s ritual site, and the resident necromancer might interrupt the taming process if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Chestnut Horse

This horse can be found east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), along the path leading towards [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp"). It's off of the north side of the road, just under halfway from Helgen to the Falkreath Stormcloak Camp.

### Find and tame the Dapple Brown Horse

This horse can be found in the forest south of [Solitude Sawmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill"), across the river but before you reach the [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mound "Skyrim:Dragon Mound"). This can obviously be a dangerous place to tame a horse if the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") is still nearby.

### Find and tame the Grey Spotted Horse

This horse can be found up the hill to the north of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm"). Beware the nearby [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") who will attack you and the horse if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Pale Mare

This horse can be found among a group of snowy pines just south of [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow").

### Find and tame the Red Horse

This horse can be found on the plains of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), northwest of [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"). It is a very easy mount to locate and tame, particularly at the start of the game.

### Find and tame the White Spotted Horse

This horse can be found directly west of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), west of the road, on a green cliff overlooking the volcanic tundra below.

## Notes

- Each wild horse can be [named](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Horse_NamingCC "Skyrim:Horses") and [saddled](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#SaddlesCC "Skyrim:Horses"), which are two other mechanics added by this Creation. To do this, you must visit a stable with the horse as your active mount.
- Horses on even slight inclines will sometimes throw you further than expected, possibly causing significant damage or killing you.

## Quest Stages

| Horse Whisperer (ccBGSSSE034\_WildHorsesQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | Hostlers in Skyrim have begun taming wild horses in order to keep up with the demand. I should speak with a hostler and see if they can give me some information. Perhaps I could find and tame some of them myself. *Objective 0:* Purchase a map of wild horse locations |
| 10 | ☑ | I've acquired a map and a journal with locations of where wild horses have been known to roam. I should find and tame them. Afterward I can bring them to a stable to add a saddle or change their name. |

| 0 |  | Find the horse. *Objective 0:* Find and tame the Chestnut Horse |
