Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted`.

Locate and tame wild horses

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to a [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").
2. Purchase a map and book for 250 gold.
3. *(Optional)* Track down and [tame](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") all seven wild horses.

### Horse Tamer

Upon reading *[Soran's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Soran%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Soran's Journal")* located on [Urag gro-Shub's](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") desk in [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"), this quest will automatically begin and will direct you to the nearest [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").[*verification needed — how is this selected?*] You will need to speak with the hostler, i.e. the NPC who sells [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). (NOTE: I received the opportunity at the Whiterun Stables in a new game to buy the map without performing any of the actions previously outlined.) You will be presented with the option to purchase a wild horse map for 250 gold. You will receive both a [Map of Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Map of Wild Horses") and a book called *[Wild Horse Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse_Notes "Skyrim:Wild Horse Notes")*. In conjunction with reading the book, the map can be examined in your inventory in order to locate seven [wild horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse "Skyrim:Wild Horse").

Upon making this purchase, this quest will conclude. However, you will then receive seven miscellaneous objectives tasking you with locating and [taming](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") every wild horse. The objectives themselves are rather useless as they do not provide a map marker for the individual horses. Instead, you will need to use the map and book to travel to the approximate location and search for the horse. The book itself advises that [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") will be useful in carrying out this task. Note that wild horses will flee if you get too close, so it may help to sneak up on them.

To tame a wild horse, you must remain mounted on the horse while it bucks. It has a chance to ragdoll you when bucking, which will force you to chase down the fleeing horse once you get back on your feet. [Sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") can help prevent the horse from fleeing too far. Once mounted for a sufficient length of time, the horse becomes an owned mount. If you switch to a different mount, it will slowly make its way back to the location you originally found it.

### Find and tame the Black Horse

This horse can be found northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), just south of the map marker for [Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove"). The book refers to nearby ruins, the ruins in question being Cracked Tusk Keep. This location is close to a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer")'s ritual site, and the resident necromancer might interrupt the taming process if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Chestnut Horse

This horse can be found east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), along the path leading towards [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp"). It's off of the north side of the road, just under halfway from Helgen to the Falkreath Stormcloak Camp.

### Find and tame the Dapple Brown Horse

This horse can be found in the forest south of [Solitude Sawmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill"), across the river but before you reach the [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mound "Skyrim:Dragon Mound"). This can obviously be a dangerous place to tame a horse if the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") is still nearby.

### Find and tame the Grey Spotted Horse

This horse can be found up the hill to the north of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm"). Beware the nearby [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") who will attack you and the horse if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Pale Mare

This horse can be found among a group of snowy pines just south of [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow").

### Find and tame the Red Horse

This horse can be found on the plains of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), northwest of [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"). It is a very easy mount to locate and tame, particularly at the start of the game.

### Find and tame the White Spotted Horse

This horse can be found directly west of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), west of the road, on a green cliff overlooking the volcanic tundra below.

## Notes

- Each wild horse can be [named](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Horse_NamingCC "Skyrim:Horses") and [saddled](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#SaddlesCC "Skyrim:Horses"), which are two other mechanics added by this Creation. To do this, you must visit a stable with the horse as your active mount.
- Horses on even slight inclines will sometimes throw you further than expected, possibly causing significant damage or killing you.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted`.

(NOTE: I received the opportunity at the Whiterun Stables in a new game to buy the map without performing any of the actions previously outlined.) You will be presented with the option to purchase a wild horse map for 250 gold. You will receive both a [Map of Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Map of Wild Horses") and a book called *[Wild Horse Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse_Notes "Skyrim:Wild Horse Notes")*. In conjunction with reading the book, the map can be examined in your inventory in order to locate seven [wild horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse "Skyrim:Wild Horse").

Upon making this purchase, this quest will conclude. However, you will then receive seven miscellaneous objectives tasking you with locating and [taming](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") every wild horse. The objectives themselves are rather useless as they do not provide a map marker for the individual horses. Instead, you will need to use the map and book to travel to the approximate location and search for the horse. The book itself advises that [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") will be useful in carrying out this task. Note that wild horses will flee if you get too close, so it may help to sneak up on them.

To tame a wild horse, you must remain mounted on the horse while it bucks. It has a chance to ragdoll you when bucking, which will force you to chase down the fleeing horse once you get back on your feet. [Sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") can help prevent the horse from fleeing too far. Once mounted for a sufficient length of time, the horse becomes an owned mount. If you switch to a different mount, it will slowly make its way back to the location you originally found it.

### Find and tame the Black Horse

This horse can be found northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), just south of the map marker for [Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove"). The book refers to nearby ruins, the ruins in question being Cracked Tusk Keep. This location is close to a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer")'s ritual site, and the resident necromancer might interrupt the taming process if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Chestnut Horse

This horse can be found east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), along the path leading towards [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp"). It's off of the north side of the road, just under halfway from Helgen to the Falkreath Stormcloak Camp.

### Find and tame the Dapple Brown Horse

This horse can be found in the forest south of [Solitude Sawmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill"), across the river but before you reach the [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mound "Skyrim:Dragon Mound"). This can obviously be a dangerous place to tame a horse if the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") is still nearby.

### Find and tame the Grey Spotted Horse

This horse can be found up the hill to the north of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm"). Beware the nearby [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") who will attack you and the horse if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Pale Mare

This horse can be found among a group of snowy pines just south of [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow").

### Find and tame the Red Horse

This horse can be found on the plains of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), northwest of [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"). It is a very easy mount to locate and tame, particularly at the start of the game.

### Find and tame the White Spotted Horse

This horse can be found directly west of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), west of the road, on a green cliff overlooking the volcanic tundra below.

## Notes

- Each wild horse can be [named](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Horse_NamingCC "Skyrim:Horses") and [saddled](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#SaddlesCC "Skyrim:Horses"), which are two other mechanics added by this Creation. To do this, you must visit a stable with the horse as your active mount.
- Horses on even slight inclines will sometimes throw you further than expected, possibly causing significant damage or killing you.

## Quest Stages

| Horse Whisperer (ccBGSSSE034\_WildHorsesQuest) | | |

| 10 | ☑ | I've acquired a map and a journal with locations of where wild horses have been known to roam. I should find and tame them. Afterward I can bring them to a stable to add a saddle or change their name. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted`.

# Skyrim:Horse Whisperer

Locate and tame wild horses

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to a [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").
2. Purchase a map and book for 250 gold.
3. *(Optional)* Track down and [tame](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") all seven wild horses.

### Horse Tamer

Upon reading *[Soran's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Soran%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Soran's Journal")* located on [Urag gro-Shub's](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") desk in [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"), this quest will automatically begin and will direct you to the nearest [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").[*verification needed — how is this selected?*] You will need to speak with the hostler, i.e. the NPC who sells [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). (NOTE: I received the opportunity at the Whiterun Stables in a new game to buy the map without performing any of the actions previously outlined.) You will be presented with the option to purchase a wild horse map for 250 gold. You will receive both a [Map of Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Map of Wild Horses") and a book called *[Wild Horse Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse_Notes "Skyrim:Wild Horse Notes")*. In conjunction with reading the book, the map can be examined in your inventory in order to locate seven [wild horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse "Skyrim:Wild Horse").

Upon making this purchase, this quest will conclude. However, you will then receive seven miscellaneous objectives tasking you with locating and [taming](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") every wild horse. The objectives themselves are rather useless as they do not provide a map marker for the individual horses. Instead, you will need to use the map and book to travel to the approximate location and search for the horse. The book itself advises that [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") will be useful in carrying out this task. Note that wild horses will flee if you get too close, so it may help to sneak up on them.

To tame a wild horse, you must remain mounted on the horse while it bucks. It has a chance to ragdoll you when bucking, which will force you to chase down the fleeing horse once you get back on your feet. [Sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") can help prevent the horse from fleeing too far. Once mounted for a sufficient length of time, the horse becomes an owned mount. If you switch to a different mount, it will slowly make its way back to the location you originally found it.

### Find and tame the Black Horse

This horse can be found northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), just south of the map marker for [Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove"). The book refers to nearby ruins, the ruins in question being Cracked Tusk Keep. This location is close to a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer")'s ritual site, and the resident necromancer might interrupt the taming process if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Chestnut Horse

This horse can be found east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), along the path leading towards [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp"). It's off of the north side of the road, just under halfway from Helgen to the Falkreath Stormcloak Camp.

### Find and tame the Dapple Brown Horse

This horse can be found in the forest south of [Solitude Sawmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill"), across the river but before you reach the [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mound "Skyrim:Dragon Mound"). This can obviously be a dangerous place to tame a horse if the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") is still nearby.

### Find and tame the Grey Spotted Horse

This horse can be found up the hill to the north of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm"). Beware the nearby [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") who will attack you and the horse if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Pale Mare

This horse can be found among a group of snowy pines just south of [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow").

### Find and tame the Red Horse

This horse can be found on the plains of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), northwest of [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"). It is a very easy mount to locate and tame, particularly at the start of the game.

### Find and tame the White Spotted Horse

This horse can be found directly west of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), west of the road, on a green cliff overlooking the volcanic tundra below.

## Notes

- Each wild horse can be [named](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Horse_NamingCC "Skyrim:Horses") and [saddled](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#SaddlesCC "Skyrim:Horses"), which are two other mechanics added by this Creation. To do this, you must visit a stable with the horse as your active mount.
- Horses on even slight inclines will sometimes throw you further than expected, possibly causing significant damage or killing you.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted`.

Locate and tame wild horses

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to a [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").
2. Purchase a map and book for 250 gold.
3. *(Optional)* Track down and [tame](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") all seven wild horses.

### Horse Tamer

(NOTE: I received the opportunity at the Whiterun Stables in a new game to buy the map without performing any of the actions previously outlined.) You will receive both a [Map of Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Map of Wild Horses") and a book called *[Wild Horse Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse_Notes "Skyrim:Wild Horse Notes")*. It's off of the north side of the road, just under halfway from Helgen to the Falkreath Stormcloak Camp.

This can obviously be a dangerous place to tame a horse if the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") is still nearby.

### Find and tame the Grey Spotted Horse

This horse can be found up the hill to the north of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm"). Beware the nearby [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") who will attack you and the horse if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Red Horse

This horse can be found on the plains of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), northwest of [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"). It is a very easy mount to locate and tame, particularly at the start of the game.

### Find and tame the White Spotted Horse

This horse can be found directly west of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), west of the road, on a green cliff overlooking the volcanic tundra below.

## Notes

- Each wild horse can be [named](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Horse_NamingCC "Skyrim:Horses") and [saddled](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#SaddlesCC "Skyrim:Horses"), which are two other mechanics added by this Creation. To do this, you must visit a stable with the horse as your active mount.
- Horses on even slight inclines will sometimes throw you further than expected, possibly causing significant damage or killing you.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted`.

# Skyrim:Horse Whisperer

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Purchase a map that lets you find wild horses.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading [Soran's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Soran%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Soran's Journal") |
| Location(s): | [The Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") |
| Reward: | [Map of Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Map of Wild Horses"), [Wild Horse Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse_Notes "Skyrim:Wild Horse Notes") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE034\_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse01\_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse02\_Black, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse03\_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse04\_Pale, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse05\_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse06\_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034\_Misc\_Horse07\_BrownSpotted |
| Added by: | [Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses") |

Locate and tame wild horses

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to a [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").
2. Purchase a map and book for 250 gold.
3. *(Optional)* Track down and [tame](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") all seven wild horses.

### Horse Tamer

Upon reading *[Soran's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Soran%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Soran's Journal")* located on [Urag gro-Shub's](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") desk in [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"), this quest will automatically begin and will direct you to the nearest [stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables").[*verification needed — how is this selected?*] You will need to speak with the hostler, i.e. the NPC who sells [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). (NOTE: I received the opportunity at the Whiterun Stables in a new game to buy the map without performing any of the actions previously outlined.) You will be presented with the option to purchase a wild horse map for 250 gold. You will receive both a [Map of Wild Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Map of Wild Horses") and a book called *[Wild Horse Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse_Notes "Skyrim:Wild Horse Notes")*. In conjunction with reading the book, the map can be examined in your inventory in order to locate seven [wild horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horse "Skyrim:Wild Horse").

Upon making this purchase, this quest will conclude. However, you will then receive seven miscellaneous objectives tasking you with locating and [taming](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Tamable_HorsesCC "Skyrim:Horses") every wild horse. The objectives themselves are rather useless as they do not provide a map marker for the individual horses. Instead, you will need to use the map and book to travel to the approximate location and search for the horse. The book itself advises that [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") will be useful in carrying out this task. Note that wild horses will flee if you get too close, so it may help to sneak up on them.

To tame a wild horse, you must remain mounted on the horse while it bucks. It has a chance to ragdoll you when bucking, which will force you to chase down the fleeing horse once you get back on your feet. [Sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") can help prevent the horse from fleeing too far. Once mounted for a sufficient length of time, the horse becomes an owned mount. If you switch to a different mount, it will slowly make its way back to the location you originally found it.

### Find and tame the Black Horse

This horse can be found northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), just south of the map marker for [Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove"). The book refers to nearby ruins, the ruins in question being Cracked Tusk Keep. This location is close to a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer")'s ritual site, and the resident necromancer might interrupt the taming process if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Chestnut Horse

This horse can be found east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), along the path leading towards [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp"). It's off of the north side of the road, just under halfway from Helgen to the Falkreath Stormcloak Camp.

### Find and tame the Dapple Brown Horse

This horse can be found in the forest south of [Solitude Sawmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill"), across the river but before you reach the [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mound "Skyrim:Dragon Mound"). This can obviously be a dangerous place to tame a horse if the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") is still nearby.

### Find and tame the Grey Spotted Horse

This horse can be found up the hill to the north of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm"). Beware the nearby [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") who will attack you and the horse if you get too close.

### Find and tame the Pale Mare

This horse can be found among a group of snowy pines just south of [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow").

### Find and tame the Red Horse

This horse can be found on the plains of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), northwest of [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"). It is a very easy mount to locate and tame, particularly at the start of the game.

### Find and tame the White Spotted Horse

This horse can be found directly west of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), west of the road, on a green cliff overlooking the volcanic tundra below.

## Notes

- Each wild horse can be [named](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#Horse_NamingCC "Skyrim:Horses") and [saddled](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses#SaddlesCC "Skyrim:Horses"), which are two other mechanics added by this Creation. To do this, you must visit a stable with the horse as your active mount.
- Horses on even slight inclines will sometimes throw you further than expected, possibly causing significant damage or killing you.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted`.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE034_WildHorsesQuest, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse01_Chestnut, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse02_Black, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse03_GreyBlack, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse04_Pale, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse05_RedBrown, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse06_WhiteSpotted, ccBGSSSE034_Misc_Horse07_BrownSpotted`.

# Skyrim:House Gray-Mane

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

House Gray-Mane

**House Gray-Mane** is the home of [Clan Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Gray-Mane") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

It is located in the Wind District, opposite the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") tree. It is the first house on the left, at the top of the stairs leading up from the marketplace.

## Residents

| Residents | Relation |
| --- | --- |
| [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane") | Patriarch |
| [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane") | Wife |
| [Avulstein Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Avulstein_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Avulstein Gray-Mane")\* | Son |
| [Olfina Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane") | Daughter |

*\** This person no longer available in this house after completing quest [Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action").

## Related Quests

- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

### Exterior

It has a fenced area beside the house, where their [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") lives. Once you have completed the reputation quest for Whiterun, in the corner is one of three barrels in the city marked with the  "Cache") Cache [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). The house has two entrances at the front and rear of the property. At the front there is a  "Loot") Loot shadowmark at the bottom of the left-hand wooden carving that flanks the front door.

| Plants | Animals |
| --- | --- |
| 1 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") | 1 [Cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") |

### House Gray-Mane

Completing the related [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action") gains you the friendship of the clan, especially [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane"), who will continue to thank you every time you speak to her for the rest of the game. It allows you to take all low value items and use all the beds from within the home freely.

The main room inside the Gray-Mane residence

The house contains many items of fancy crockery and many sacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") throughout. Entering through the front door leads directly into a central room with a large fire pit in front of you. To the right of this is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand, with a low table and two chairs behind the fire. On the table is a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a common book. On your right, in the eastern corner is a set of shelves holding crockery and flanked by two chairs. To the left is a small wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a crate with two wall shelves above. In front of these is a flight of wooden stairs leading up to the partially boarded upper floor. In the northern corner is a set of shelves holding four common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), a cheese wheel, a bowl containing ten [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs, and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). To the left of this is a doorway to a storage area either side of the rear door. Further to the left along the northwest wall is a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes.

At the southwestern end of the room is a large wooden table with three chairs situated on each side of it. On the table are two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a gourd, a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), and a bowl containing [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). Against the southwest wall is a narrow table holding a bowl of green apples and a platter filled with a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") and a bulb of garlic. To the left of the large table is a set of shelves holding three bottles of wine and beside this is a food barrel and a crate with a sweet roll on top. The storage area, either side of the rear door has two wall shelves to the left, over a pile of firewood and a cupboard, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a [fish barrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Fish_Barrel "Skyrim:Containers") to the right. On the cupboard shelves are a couple of pieces of cheese, while the chest contains only minor loot.

Fralia's bedroom

In the middle of the northeast wall is a pair of wooden doors leading into [Eorlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane") and [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane")'s bedroom. It contains a large double bed coming out from the northeast wall with end tables on either side. Against the north wall is a narrow table holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bowl containing three honey nut treats, while against the northwest wall is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with an unlocked chest and a piece of cheese on top. In the southern corner is a round wooden table and two chairs, set for two, holding a bottle of alto wine, two more honey nut treats and a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat").

At the top of the stairs you will see that the upper floor has been boarded in a horse shoe balcony overlooking downstairs with two doors off of it; one immediately on your left and the other opposite at the northeastern end of the house. The first room is a bedroom containing a single bed, behind the door in the eastern corner of the room, with an end table beside it and a wedge of cheese on top. Against the southeast wall is a dresser with a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and a [silver sapphire necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Sapphire_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Sapphire Necklace") on top, a wash basin to the left and a chair to the right. Against the northwest wall is a small cupboard with a set of fine clothes on top and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots") beside it. To the northeast on the other side of the door is a large cupboard holding a bowl of [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a small table to the left with a jug on top.

On the balcony, to the right of the bedroom is a tall wardrobe and further along the southwest wall is a small cupboard with a bottle of wine on top. In the western corner is a chair with three bookcases to the right, along the northwest wall. There are twenty common books and a bottle of wine on the shelves. In the northern corner is a low table with a bottle of wine on top and a chair beside it and two unlocked chests against the northeast wall separated by a small partition. To the right of the second of these is a set of shelves holding two bottles of Nord mead. At the end of the balcony is a large wooden table and two chairs, with a bottle of ale and a bowl containing three potatoes.

Between the shelves and table is the second door leading to another bedroom, this containing a large four-posted double bed with an end table on either side and an unlocked chest at the foot of the bed. On the end table on the left is a bottle of Nord mead and a [silver emerald necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Emerald_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Emerald Necklace"). Either side of the door is a tall wardrobe and wash basin to the left and a dresser with a set of clothes on top and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") beside.

## Notes

- Although he is absent, [Thorald Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") is also a member of Clan Gray-Mane. Ordinarily he would live in the house with the rest of his family and carry a piece of [Skyforge Steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel") weaponry.

## Bugs

- If you face the north corner with the small red plant formation and walk into the plant, you will clip through the ground. **?**

House of Clan Battle-Born

**House of Clan Battle-Born** is the home to Clan [Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born "Skyrim:Battle-Born").

It is located in the Wind District of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), next to the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)"). Across the street is the house of the Battle-Born's rivals, Clan [Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Gray-Mane").

## Residents

| Residents | Relation |
| --- | --- |
| [Olfrid Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born") | Patriarch |
| [Bergritte Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Bergritte_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Bergritte Battle-Born") | Wife |
| [Jon Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Jon_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Jon Battle-Born") | Son |
| [Alfhild Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Alfhild_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Alfhild Battle-Born") | Daughter |
| [Idolaf Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Idolaf_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Idolaf Battle-Born") | Married to Alfhild |
| [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born") | Son of Idolaf and Alfhild |

## Related Quests

- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There are two entrances to the house, the main door is up a flight of stone stairs and is often novice-locked, while the rear door is often unlocked. To the left of the property are three wooden benches surrounding a lit brazier. There are a couple of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") bushes near the house.

### House of Clan Battle-Born

The main reception room

Entering through the front door, leads into the main room, with a large fire pit in the center and a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") directly in front of you. On your left, in the western corner is a bookcase, two low chairs and a low table. On the bookcase are a selection of common books, several [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") that are found throughout the home along with, a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") of [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), and a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") holding two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and a tomato. Beside it is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack. On the table is a bowl containing a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). Along the northwest wall is a long end table with a bowl containing two [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") on top and a wooden bench to the right and further to the right of the bench is a wooden door into Olfrid's bedroom. On the other side of the door is a narrow table holding a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") on a plate and another bowl of tomatoes. In the northern corner is a cupboard holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), with a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot, coming along the northeast wall.

In the middle of the northeast wall is the rear entrance and in the eastern corner is a set of shelves holding more household items, a couple of bottles of alto wine and a couple more common books. Either side of the shelves is a chair. Against the southeast wall is a small unit holding a bowl of [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup") and a common book. To the right of this is a wooden door into Lars' bedroom, with a wooden bench to the right and a doorway beyond, that leads to the stairs and the top floor. To the right of the doorway, in the southern corner is a square wooden table and two chairs, on the table is an unlocked chest holding minor loot, two goblets and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). On the far side of the fire pit from the main entrance is a chair and small table pulled close to the fire. On this table is a bowl containing a goat cheese wedge and a goblet and between that and the rear door is a table laid for six people. On the table are six plates, with an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), a loaf of bread, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), two bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a bottle of Nord mead and a bottle of alto wine.

[Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born")'s room is L-shaped and consists of an owned child's bed in the southern corner with an end table beside it. Opposite the bed, next to the door is a tall wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), jewelry and clutter. At the southeast end of the room there is a bookcase in the eastern corner holding five common books. Against the southwest wall is a long end table and chair with more common books, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") on top.

Olfrid's spacious bedroom

[Olfrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born") and [Bergritte Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Bergritte_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Bergritte Battle-Born")'s bedroom consists of a king-sized four-poster bed, with an end table either side. On these is a [silver jeweled necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Jeweled_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Jeweled Necklace"), a copy of *[The Cake and The Diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cake_and_The_Diamond "Skyrim:The Cake and The Diamond")*, two goblets and a bowl containing two honey nut treats. Against the southeast wall is a dresser with a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), two cups, a bowl containing a gourd and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots") on top. To the right against the southwest corner is a set of shelves holding a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Battle of Sancre Tor](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Sancre_Tor "Skyrim:Battle of Sancre Tor")*, several household items, a green apple, and a copy of *[Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Harvesting_Frostbite_Spider_Venom "Skyrim:Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom")*. Against the northwest wall is a small unit holding a [silver ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina") and more household items. In the southwest corner of the room is a door into Olfrid’s study.

Olfrid's study

The study consists of a chair against the northwest wall, behind the door. In the western corner is a bookcase with eight common books, a copy of *[Imperial Report on Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Report_on_Saarthal "Skyrim:Imperial Report on Saarthal")*, a loaf of bread, with a small unit to the left holding more common books, a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a bowl of bread and other household items. Against the southeast wall is a large desk and chair, with a small wardrobe containing fine clothes underneath on the left. On the desk is a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a potion of healing, two silver ingots, a plate with two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat") on and if you have started the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action") an *[Imperial Missive](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Missive_(Battle-Born) "Skyrim:Imperial Missive (Battle-Born)")*. Above the desk are two wall shelves holding a silver ingot and a food sack, with another sack under the desk.

Through the doorway to the stairs, on the left against the northeast wall is a cupboard with a sack on top. In the southern corner, against the southwest wall is a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes and against the southeast wall is a wooden bench. The stairs are opposite the wardrobe and have several crates and sacks underneath, with a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on one of the crates. At the top of the stair is a small wardrobe with a bowl containing a sweet roll, a bottle of wine. The top floor is only partially floored out, with an area beside the stairs floored across the width of the house creating a sitting area, with a large round wooden table and two chairs. On the table are two plates, a baked potato, a portion of grilled leeks, an apple pie, a common book and a bottle of wine. Against the southwest eaves is a long end table holding a platter containing two potatoes, a tomato, a goat cheese wedge and four salmon steaks.

Idolaf and Alfhild's bedroom

The flooring continues along the northeastern edge of the house, past a narrow table holding several pieces of goat cheese and [Jon Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Jon_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Jon Battle-Born")'s large bedroom on the right. [Idolaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Idolaf_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Idolaf Battle-Born") and [Alfhild Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Alfhild_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Alfhild Battle-Born")'s large, well-appointed bedroom can be found at the end of the hall. That consists of a king-sized bed coming out from the middle of the northwest wall, with an end table on each side. On the end tables is a bowl containing four portions of grilled leeks, a bottle of [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison"), a goblet and a plate with an apple pie on top. At the foot of the bed is an unlocked long chest containing minor loot. There is another long end table in the western corner of the room. On top of this table is a plate filled with two baked potatoes, a bottle of alto wine and a couple of common books, there is also another plate underneath the end table. In the south corner is a square wooden table and two chairs. On the table are two plates, one holding an apple pie, while the other holds a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), also on the table is a potion of healing and a bottle of alto wine. There is a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes against the southeast wall with a couple of sacks on the floor beside it. Against the northeast wall is a cupboard, a low table with a bowl of bottles of Nord mead and a washbasin.

Jon's bedroom

Jon's bedroom consists of a king-sized bed coming out from under the eaves to the southeast with a small low table on each side, these hold a common book and bottle of alto wine. In the eastern corner is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). On top is a [philter of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Philter of Resist Fire"), a bowl of boiled creme treats, and a bottle of alto wine. In the middle of the northeast wall is a small square wooden table and two chairs. On the table are a couple of plates, two bottles of Nord mead, a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat") and a piece of cheese with an open crate containing a worthless jug and five bottles of Nord mead. The northern corner has small set of shelves, on these shelves are five common books, a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and bottle of alto wine, with a sack beside it. The center of the northwest eaves has a long wooden table against it. This has a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"), a potion of plentiful stamina and a bottle of alto wine on it. To the left of the table is a bookcase with several common books strewn on the floor in front of it and on the shelves. On your right as you enter this room is an unlocked chest containing more minor loot.

## Notes

- There is a  "Protected") Protected [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the left of the front door, near the ground and to the right of the back door. [Olfrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born") pledges the full support of the Battle-Born clan to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") once [Imitation Amnesty](/wiki/Skyrim:Imitation_Amnesty "Skyrim:Imitation Amnesty") has been completed.

## Bugs

- Despite the Protected shadowmark, you can still be required to steal items from this house by the Thieves Guild, as part of [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex")'s radiant thievery jobs.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, addresses this issue. The house is no longer a valid quest target.

# Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: House of Clan Cruel-Sea ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=House+of+Clan+Cruel-Sea)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |

The House of Clan Cruel-Sea

The **House of Clan Cruel-Sea** is a large manor house that is the home of the Cruel-Sea family, in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

It is located opposite [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim"), in the northwestern area of the city.

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Grimvar Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimvar_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Grimvar Cruel-Sea")  [Hillevi Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillevi_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Hillevi Cruel-Sea")  [Torsten Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Torsten Cruel-Sea")  [Idesa Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Idesa_Sadri "Skyrim:Idesa Sadri") |

## Related Quests

- **[Summerset Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows")**: Remove a rival guild from the picture.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## House of Clan Cruel-Sea

Ground floor, with dining area

There is a square arch to pass under to approach this large fancy house, it is the largest house in Windhelm excluding the palace and contains numerous bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") along with fancy [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), [jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks. There are three food barrels to the left of the entrance and several mountain flowers planted in and around the front yard area. The front door is generally novice-locked. Entering leads into a large room with a long wooden table with benches either side directly in front of you. Against the east wall is a small wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a long end table. There is a doorway to the north with a small unit to the right. Against the west wall is a set of shelves holding a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing").

Through the doorway is another large room with a set of shelves against the east wall. To the north is an alcove with a tall wardrobe, several crates and cupboard holding a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"). There are a row of four weapon racks on the south wall and stairs leading up to the east against the north wall. The western end of the room is given over to use as a kitchen with a fireplace with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a long wooden table. There is an alcove to the south with a small set of shelves with a long wooden table with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top. To the right is a cupboard containing clutter. To the right of the fireplace is a pile of firewood. In an alcove opposite the one to the south is a large vat, three food barrels and a couple of chairs. To the right are the stairs to the second floor.

Upstairs firepit

At the top of the stairs is a large room with a central firepit with a chimney surround and a low table by the top of the stairs with a [silver emerald necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Emerald_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Emerald Necklace") on top. Against the north wall is a small set of shelves with a long table to the right with [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). There is another set of shelves to the east with a wooden bench with chairs flanking it to the right. In the southeastern corner is a large round table holding [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield") and a [draught of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Draught of Lasting Potency"). To the right is a doorway with a second doorway to the southwest. Against the south wall are yet another set of shelves and to the west shelves, with another wooden bench to the right.

Southern bedrooms areas

Through the doorway to the southwest is a bedroom consists of a single bed in the southwestern corner, a small unit holding a [draught of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health") and a [draught of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Draught of Regeneration"), a low table and an end table all to the south. To the north is a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes to the right of a doorway to another bedroom. This bedroom is used by [Torsten Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Torsten Cruel-Sea") and consists of a single bed against the north wall, a tall wardrobe, long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot and a small set of shelves holding a potion of minor stamina, a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") and copies of *[2920, First Seed, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_First_Seed,_v3 "Skyrim:2920, First Seed, v3")* and *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* all against the east wall. Against the south wall, to the left of the doorway is a small unit holding a draught of health, a draught of regeneration. To the right of the doorway is an end table holding a leather strip. There is a wash basin in the northwest corner and a round wooden table near the middle of the room.

Torsten's bedroom

The doorway to the south from the room with the firepit in leads to two further bedroom, the first has a doorway to the second, immediately on the left as you enter the first. The first bedroom contains a single bed against the south wall. A tall wardrobe and wash basin are against the east wall. In the southwest corner is a pair of shelves holding a [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength") and a draught of health. Against the west wall is a large wooden table. Next to the doorway is a bookcase that is empty.

The final bedroom is used by [Idesa Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Idesa_Sadri "Skyrim:Idesa Sadri") and consists of a single bed against the east wall, with a set of shelves to the left holding a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and having a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") in front of them on the floor. Against the south wall is a small wardrobe with shelves above holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a leather strip, with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") leaning against them. In the southwest corner is a pair of shelves holding a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina") and a [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"). Against the west wall is a wash basin and tall wardrobe containing fine clothes. Finally in the northwest corner, next to the doorway is an end table.

## Notes

- There is a  "Protected") Protected [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the top left of the entrance door and another on the bottom right pillar of the archway before the house.

## Bugs

- The arrangement of the beds is set incorrectly for the number of adults (3) and children (1) living here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12012)) One of the child beds is now an adult bed, and Grimvar's bed is now marked as owned by him.
- Despite the  "Protected") Protected shadowmarks, you can still be required to steal items from this house by the Thieves Guild, as part of [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex")'s radiant thievery jobs.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=15875)) The house is no longer a valid quest target.

# Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield

## Overview

House of Clan Shatter-Shield

**House of Clan Shatter-Shield** is a large house on the western wall of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). Opposite [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House"), next door to [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") which was formerly owned by their other daughter Friga Shatter-Shield.

It is home to [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield"), his wife [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield") and daughter [Nilsine Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield"). All of whom are mourning the loss of their other daughter/sister Friga who died at the hand of a murderer, who you can find by completing [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice").

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Nilsine Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield")  [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield")  [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield") |

## Related Quests

- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

## House of Clan Shatter-Shield

The yard in front and to the sides of the house contain nothing of interest. Upon entering through the expert-locked entrance you enter into a dining room with a long wooden table with benches either side in the center, doorways to the south and in the northeastern corner. Small units either side of the entrance, with the one on the left holding a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). The other on the right holds a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") and three more bottles of wine--(see [notes](#Notes)). To the right of the doorway to the south is another small unit holding another bowl. The table is laid with various high quality [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), bowls and [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") as well as two bottles of wine and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). To the right of the doorway in the northeastern corner are a couple of barrels with a set of shelves holding more bottles of wine and alto wine to the right of these.

Tova's bedroom

The doorway to the south leads into [Tova Shatter-Shield's](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield") bedroom which consists of a single owned bed in an alcove to the east, with a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") by the head of the bed. Against the south wall is a set of shelves holding a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and a bottle of wine, with a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") in front of it. Further along the wall are a stack of crates and sack containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). There is a wash basin against the west wall with a large round wooden table and a chair further to the right. On the table is a bottle of wine, a bowl and goblet. Against the north wall is a tall wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") beside the doorway.

Through the other doorway, to the north is a kitchen area with a flight of stairs up to the second story against the west wall, climbing to the south. On your right against the south wall as you enter this area are a series of small units holding a bowl, a jug and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), with a small firepit to the east with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") over it. Against the north wall is a larger firepit with a non functioning cooking spit over it, with a narrow wooden table holding several food sacks to the left.

House of the Shatter-Shield clan

Climbing the stairs bring you to a sitting room with a small unit holding two bottles of Nord mead against you the south wall in front of you at the top of the stairs. To the east is a large fireplace with a couple of low chairs pulled up in front of it and a small set of shelves in an alcove to the right holding a bottle of Nord mead. To the left of the fireplace is a pile of firewood and by this, against the north wall is a set of shelves holding a goblet. There are two doorways from this room, one to the north and the other opposite to the south, they both lead to bedrooms.
[Nilsine Shatter-Shield's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield") bedroom to the north contains a single bed along the north wall with a corner shelf holding a drum to the left and a tall wardrobe containing fine clothes to the right. In front of this is a wash basin, with a small wardrobe to the east and further to the right in an alcove is a set of shelves holding an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") and a bottle of Nord mead. In the southeast corner of the room is a large round wooden table and chair, with a plate, goblet and bottle of Nord mead on the table. Against the west wall is a low chair, a couple of barrels, several sacks and a crate beside another set of shelves. These hold another bottle of Nord mead.

Nilsine's room

The other bedroom, to the south is used by [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield") and contains a single bed coming out from the east wall with a small unit to the right, with a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on the floor in front of it. Against the south wall is a tall wardrobe, a wash basin, a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and in the southwest corner a large round wooden table and chair, with a plate on the table. Against the west wall are a stack of crates and to the right a set of shelves holding a sack of food, with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") leaning against it. In the northwest corner is another sack and barrel. In the northeast corner is another corner shelf, with a small wardrobe to the left and a set of shelves further left, by the doorway these hold a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe").

After completing a Dark Brotherhood [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes"), if you decide to include [Nilsine Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield"), when you next enter the home you will find [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield") sleeping in the northern bedroom and [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield") laying dead on the floor beside the bed with a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova%27s_Farewell "Skyrim:Tova's Farewell") lying next to her body explaining her depression and wish to be reunited with both her daughters.

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the top right of the entrance door.
- There is a rather unique collection of undersized and oversized wine bottles in this house. However, once they are taken they stack normally in your equipment list and if dropped they will be of normal size.
  -  When playing on Xbox 360, these bottles will retain their specific sizes.
  - You can keep their unique sizes by taking them one at a time (each size at a time) and bringing them to your own house and dropping them, then coming back for more.
- There is an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") on the second floor in the northern bedroom on a set of shelves against the eastern wall. Even though its rollover text is white (like it is unowned), taking it in plain view of the Shatter-Shields will have them taking it back from you and yelling for guards. You have to be sneaking and undetected when taking the gem.

## Bugs

- The right corner of the house's exterior is not solid, allowing you to bypass the town walls.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
