Hrodulf's House

**Hrodulf's House** is an abandoned [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Places#Shacks "Skyrim:Dragonborn Places") southwest of [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth") and southeast of [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow").

It is heavily damaged, though the embers of a fire still burn in a firepit within.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Hrodulf's Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_Madness "Skyrim:Hrodulf's Madness")**: Uncover the secret of Hrodulf's House.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Unexpected house guests

Several [trama root](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root") plants and [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants dot the surrounding area, and two [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") deposits can be found east of the building. Two [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") will rise out of the ground near the caved-in wall and attack as you approach. If you climb up onto the east roof of the building, you will find an apprentice-locked strongbox containing gold and some random gems and/or jewelry.

### Hrodulf's House

The building itself is badly damaged, with holes in the walls and part of the roof missing. In fact, the whole of the northwest corner of the house has gone; the ash is piled high in the corners of the house, and most of the remaining furniture has been pushed together and jumbled up. Under the table is a bottle of [flin](/wiki/Skyrim:Flin "Skyrim:Flin"). An [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") rests on the lower shelf of a small bookcase in the northwest corner of the building, next to a larger bookcase that holds a cup and bowls, a [draught of resist magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Draught of Resist Magic"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), and an [elixir of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Health "Skyrim:Elixir of Health"). An unlocked chest against part of the south wall contains low-level loot, and to the right of the chest is a trapdoor that leads to the cellar.

### Hrodulf's House Cellar

*"Listen to this one!"*

Upon entering the cellar, you will overhear two [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") laughing as they read the [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Letter (Dragonborn)") to [Hrodulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf "Skyrim:Hrodulf") from a lover named [Bjornolfr](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjornolfr "Skyrim:Bjornolfr") asking Hrodulf to leave the island and return to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). In the northwestern corner under the stairs you enter via, behind a wooden column is a [silver necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace") among the cobwebs. On your left against the east wall is a set of shelves containing a piece of [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather"). Beside the first set of shelves is a smaller set with [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on top. There are nine [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") in the southeast corner of the room. The two reavers you can hear talking are down at the far end of the room past some bookcases that are dividing the room. Against the south wall is a narrow table with two random potions, a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), and a copy of *[The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v2 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2")*. A [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a copy of *[The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v1 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1")* are on the floor in front of the narrow table, next to a bedroll. Behind this are the two chairs that the reavers were sitting on, next to a low table holding a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two portions of [charred skeever meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Meat "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Meat"), a cooked [horse haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a [flawless amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Amethyst "Skyrim:Flawless Amethyst"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), and the letter from Bjornolfr to Hrodulf mentioned above. There are a couple sacks in the southwest corner. Against the west wall is a large box with three [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), a bottle of Nord mead, and a portion of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat") on top.

In front of the box is a firepit with a copy of *[Brief History of the Empire, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v3 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v3")* in the fire. There are also copies of *[Dwarves, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarves,_v2 "Skyrim:Dwarves, v2")*, *[Ode To The Tundrastriders](/wiki/Skyrim:Ode_To_The_Tundrastriders "Skyrim:Ode To The Tundrastriders")*, *[Dunmer of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Dunmer of Skyrim")*, *[Cats of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Cats_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Cats of Skyrim")*, *[Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Ice_Wraiths "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths")*, *[Dwemer History and Culture](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_History_and_Culture "Skyrim:Dwemer History and Culture")*, *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")*, and two random books beside the firepit scattered on the floor. To the right of the firepit is a moveable bookcase. There are two barrels and an unlocked chest against the northern wall, with a second bedroll on the floor in front. Near this bedroll is a random helmet and a crate with [Hrodulf's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hrodulf's Journal") on top, with a third barrel against the east wall.

Treasure

Activating the bookshelf on the west wall will reveal a tunnel (mentioned in Hrodulf's journal and spoken of by the reavers), which heads down to the west. At the corner where it turns to the north is a pickaxe, a shovel, a loose [coin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a unique lit [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") which is weightless and adds dynamic shadows to objects when held. In front of you are stairs leading up to a small Dwemer chamber where the machinery that helped to drive Hrodulf mad still operates. Inside this room is the body of Bjornolfr, apparently killed by the reavers. His inventory includes a [novice hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Hood "Skyrim:Novice Hood") and [novice robes of Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Robes_of_Conjuration "Skyrim:Novice Robes of Conjuration"), as well as a [bloodstained letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstained_Letter "Skyrim:Bloodstained Letter"). There are four loose coins and a random dagger beside his body. To the right of Bjornolfr is an unlocked Dwemer chest. Farther into the room is a stone table and chair; on the table are three [Dwarven metal ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Metal_Ingot "Skyrim:Dwarven Metal Ingot") and a [Dwemer knife](/wiki/Skyrim:Knife_(item) "Skyrim:Knife (item)"). Behind the table is a large unlocked stone chest which, if you have been directed here by a quest to find an item, will contain the item in question. To the right of this chest is a Dwarven dresser containing a [Dwemer bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Bowl "Skyrim:Dwemer Bowl"), [fork](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_(item) "Skyrim:Fork (item)"), and [gyro](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Gyro "Skyrim:Dwemer Gyro"), while against the north wall on the floor are a [Dwemer cup](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cup "Skyrim:Dwemer Cup"), pot, and [pan](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Pan "Skyrim:Dwemer Pan").

### Hrodulf's Boat

Hrodulf's boat and body, guarded by a [burnt spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Burnt_Spriggan "Skyrim:Burnt Spriggan"), can be found by going directly south from the house to the water's edge. Next to him is a [broken iron war axe handle](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Iron_War_Axe_Handle "Skyrim:Broken Iron War Axe Handle") and a [broken iron war axe head](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Iron_War_Axe_Head "Skyrim:Broken Iron War Axe Head"). He also left behind an [amulet of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Mara "Skyrim:Amulet of Mara") and a [gold diamond ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Diamond_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Diamond Ring") on the boat seat. A chest is next to the boat, as well as an apprentice-locked strongbox and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). There are two [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") plants growing next to the body, with several more nearby.

## Bugs

- Hrodulf's body may not be present at his boat.

# Skyrim:Hrodulf's Madness

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Uncover the secret of [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | DLC2dunHrodulf |

Unwanted [visitors](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") outside [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House")

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal (see [this section](#Quest_Stages) for details).

1. Investigate [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House").
2. Fight the [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") in the cellar.
3. Uncover the secret behind the bookshelf.
4. Find out what happened to [Hrodulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf "Skyrim:Hrodulf") and [Bjornolfr](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjornolfr "Skyrim:Bjornolfr").

### Hrodulf's House

On the hill between [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth") and the [Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall") lies the charred remains of a shack called [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House"). Not much is left of the original interior and the house is seemingly uninhabited and partly covered in ash. When you approach the premises, two [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") will rise from the ashes and attack. Dispose of them and look around for some minor loot in a chest, an East Empire Company strongbox holding a [pendant](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for the quest [Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace"), and finally, a trap door leading to a secret underground basement.

### The Reavers

*"Listen to this one!"*

Downstairs, you will find a much more comfortable room, complete with a table, bookshelves, and food, but also some unwanted visitors, specifically two [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") hiding from the ash spawn you just confronted upstairs. You will land in a safe spot behind a corner, so you can overhear the conversation:

**Reaver #1**: *"Listen to this one! 'My nights have been impossible to bear without you. I beg of you: Please depart that blasted isle and return to Solitude at once!'"*
**Reaver #2**: *"Ha ha ha! No more! What a fool."*
**Reaver #1**: *"Do you think he's the one we left in the tunnel?"*
**Reaver #2**: *"Who cares? Nords all look the same to me."*
**Reaver #1**: *"Ha! Wait... Did you hear that? Sounds like those Ash Spawn are back."*
**Reaver #2**: *"Well, at least if the other Nord returns, they'll take care of him."*

After the conversation, the reavers will start walking towards you and the trapdoor, so expose yourself and battle them both. Once they are dead, investigate the table and read the [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Letter (Dragonborn)") that amused them so much.

### Follow the Clues

The letter is from a [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") citizen named [Bjornolfr](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjornolfr "Skyrim:Bjornolfr") and is addressed to his lover, [Hrodulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf "Skyrim:Hrodulf"). In the letter Bjornolfr shows great concern about the welfare of Hrodulf, and encourages him to leave [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") and return to Solitude. Look around the room and locate [Hrodulf's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hrodulf's Journal") on the crate to the north. Read through it and learn about the growing madness of newcomer Hrodulf who moved into the house, only to be obsessed with a strange rumbling from the basement, in his own words, *"a calling from the depths"*. As his madness escalated, Hrodulf went to town and bought various tools for digging, and apparently broke down a wall behind one of the bookshelves, obsessed with solving the mystery about the voices from beyond. Before the journal turns into the ramblings of a madman, Hrodulf shows concern about Bjornolfr and the possibility that he would travel to Solstheim and seek out Hrodulf in his house. Hrodulf, however, is nowhere to be found in the basement and you will have no choice but to investigate the bookshelves and find the one you can push aside.

### Fire From the Deep

What lies beneath

Behind the bookshelf is the tunnel created by Hrodulf in his desperate attempt to uncover the secret in his basement. The noises from below can be heard clearly, and as you delve underground, a small chamber reveals several [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") machines, all of them still functioning and pumping. Lying on the ground is Bjornolfr, who obviously found the journal and went down there looking for his lover, but found the two reavers instead. On his body you will find a [bloodstained letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstained_Letter "Skyrim:Bloodstained Letter"), Hrodulf's cryptic plea to Bjornolfr to stay away from the house. The chamber itself contains various dwemer artifacts, three [dwarven metal ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Metal_Ingot "Skyrim:Dwarven Metal Ingot"), two dwemer chests, one of them boss-leveled, and some gold coins scattered around. Hrodulf, however, is still missing and nothing will point you to his location.

On the coast south of Hrodulf's house, you will find a canoe and a [burnt spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Burnt_Spriggan "Skyrim:Burnt Spriggan") standing over the corpse of Hrodulf, and some rare [scrap metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots#Scrap_Metal "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots") (a Broken Iron War Axe Head and Handle). He seemingly realized his madness and tried to escape Solstheim in the canoe, but his life instead ended at the hands of a wilderness creature, having caused the death of his lover through his obsession with the strange voices.

## Notes

- The cause of madness that came from the Dwarven machinery was likely Dwemer [tonal architecture](/wiki/Lore:Tonal_Architecture "Lore:Tonal Architecture"). Depending on the usage, machines such as Dwarven tonal resonators can induce a deep calmness, profound pleasure, or paranoia and terror, with the latter being what Hrodulf experienced.

## Bugs

- Sometimes Hrodulf's body may despawn. This may be caused by his body falling through the ground.

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 10.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2dunHrodulf stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2dunHrodulf`.

# Skyrim:Hrothmund's Barrow

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Hrothmund's Barrow ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Hrothmund%27s+Barrow)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Hrothmund%27s_Barrow "Lore:Hrothmund's Barrow")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 10 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2HrothmundsBarrow01, DLC2HrothmundsBarrowExterior01 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| Southwest of [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore") | 1 |
| # of [Silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") | 1 |

Hrothmund's Barrow

**Hrothmund's Barrow** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike").

It contains the axe once wielded by [Hrothmund](/wiki/Lore:Hrothmund_the_Red "Lore:Hrothmund the Red"). During the quest [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk"), after you have helped a group of [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") clear [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") of [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"), you are sent here to witness a ritual confirming the hall's rightful leader.

## Related Quests

- **[Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk")**: Help [Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy") retake [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").

### Exterior

Hrothmund's Bane

In the open area in front of the entrance is a [pattern of large stones](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Hrothmund%27s_Bane "Bloodmoon:Hrothmund's Bane"). To the right of the entrance is an unlit brazier. [Frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") may be encountered nearby.

### Hrothmund's Barrow

The large flooded chamber

Hrothmund's Axe

The entrance leads into a natural cave with a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") and three patches of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus. A short flight of stairs ascends to the north along the west wall. At the top of the stairs, a set of iron doors is on the northeast wall, while a concealed door on the southeast wall is opened by the pull chain to the left. Beyond the concealed door is a damp twisting tunnel ending at a second concealed door opened by the pull chain to the right. Beyond this door is a small shallowly flooded chamber containing a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") and a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), with a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a [flawless garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Garnet "Skyrim:Flawless Garnet"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), and a [flawless emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Emerald "Skyrim:Flawless Emerald") next to the chest.

Returning to the area outside the first concealed door, beyond the set of iron doors is a flight of stairs descending into a large flooded chamber. As you descend the stairs, the water will drain to reveal two paths on either side of a large stone sculpture. The paths rejoin and continue to the far end of the room, where a raised platform features a stone holding Hrothmund's Axe. Two chests flank the alcove with the stone.

## Notes

- Southwest of the entrance at an [unmarked location](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Reaver.27s_End "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") is an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox").
- Northwest of the entrance are two [sapphire geodes](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Geode "Skyrim:Sapphire Geode"). Due north of the second sapphire geode above a waterfall is a chest and a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword").
- Southeast of the entrance are two sapphire geodes, a silver ore vein, and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein").
- Hrothmund's Axe is not an actual weapon, and cannot be obtained by any means.
- [Hrothmund's Barrow](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Hrothmund%27s_Barrow "Bloodmoon:Hrothmund's Barrow") previously appeared in [Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon").

# Skyrim:Hunt and Gather

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Retrieve [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah")'s [spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Spoon "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Spoon"), [ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Quest Items"), and [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Soul Gem").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah") |
| Location(s): | [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep"), [Fellstar Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm"), [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(place) "Skyrim:The White Phial (place)"), [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") |
| Reward: | 5 random high-value [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften14 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

Help Wylandriah retrieve some lost items.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah").
2. Retrieve her [spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Spoon "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Spoon").
3. Retrieve her [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Soul Gem").
4. Retrieve her [orichalcum ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Quest Items").
5. Return to Wylandriah.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After asking Wylandriah if she needs help she will enlist your aid to help retrieve some items she accidentally left behind while on her travels. She needs these implements to perform an oddly-inspired experiment. All items can be found in unique containers labeled "Wylandriah's Satchel".

### Satchel Locations

| Item | City | Building | Satchel Location | Image |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Wylandriah's Spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Spoon "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Spoon") | [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") | [Fellstar Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm") | On the table. | [On the table](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Hunt_and_Gather_02.jpg "On the table") |
| [Wylandriah's Soul Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Soul Gem") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(place) "Skyrim:The White Phial (place)") | Behind the staircase, on top of a barrel. | [Behind the staircase, on top of a barrel](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Hunt_and_Gather_03.jpg "Behind the staircase, on top of a barrel") |
| [Orichalcum Ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Quest Items") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") | [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") | On a bookshelf in the main room. | [On a bookshelf in the main room](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Hunt_and_Gather_04.jpg "On a bookshelf in the main room") |

Wylandriah's items can be acquired in any order. To find the spoon, go to Ivarstead and enter Fellstar Farm's house. Wylandriah's satchel is sitting on a table. To find the soul gem, go to The White Phial in the market in Windhelm. There are two barrels under the staircase; Wylandriah's satchel is on top of the barrel closest to the door. To find the orichalcum ingot, go to The Frozen Hearth in Winterhold right across from the [jarl's longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)"). Wylandriah's satchel is on the bookshelf with the [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") plants next to [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar")'s room. Return to Wylandriah with the items and she will give you several random [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls") as a reward, but will have no recollection of actually setting you on the task.

## Notes

- The orichalcum ingot is a special quest version found only in her satchel, but not named like the other two items.
- Fellstar Farm is locked during the day, so you may want to enter at night if you don't want to risk getting caught trespassing. Or, if you are trying to maintain a good character, you can wait until the family stops working in the garden. Then, one by one, they will enter the house. The mother is the last one to enter the house. After she enters, the house becomes unlocked, and you can enter the house without trespassing.

## Bugs

- If you pick up one of the items before engaging in the quest, Wylandriah may not ask this favor. Finding all three should trigger an update and allow them to be turned in though.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Wylandriah's Soul Gem is fillable, and despite being a quest item it can be used to recharge enchanted weapons. Using the gem to recharge enchanted weapons will consume the gem thus making the quest impossible to complete.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. Wylandriah's Soul Gem has been changed to be non-fillable.
- In some cases the items will not show up when you search the satchels, making the quest impossible to complete.

## Quest Stages

| Hunt and Gather (FreeformRiften14) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Retrieve Wylandriah's Spoon  *Objective 20:* Retrieve Wylandriah's Ingot  *Objective 30:* Retrieve Wylandriah's Soul Gem |
| 30 |  | *(Wylandriah's Spoon acquired)* |
| 40 |  | *(Wylandriah's Ingot acquired)* |
| 50 |  | *(Wylandriah's Soul Gem acquired)* |
| 60 |  | *Objective 40:* Return to Wylandriah |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften14 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften14`.

# Skyrim:Hunter's Rest

## Overview

|  |

Hunter's Rest

**Hunter's Rest** is a small shack northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

The two [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer#Elk "Skyrim:Deer") [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") who live here sell various [meats](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and [pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Hides "Skyrim:Animal Hides").

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | **Two [Hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter")** | |

## Walkthrough

Hunters resting

This cozy one-room shelter in the hills south of [Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern") provides a welcome respite for weary adventurers. Outside, you'll find a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over a campfire. Several joints of [raw venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") owned by the hunters are outside and inside the shack. An elk carcass on a table against the west wall of the shack can be freely harvested for its [hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), meat, and possibly [small](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers") or [large antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Large_Antlers "Skyrim:Large Antlers"). Next to the table is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") is on the east side of the house. A [beehive](/wiki/Skyrim:Bee "Skyrim:Bee") hangs from a flagpole east of the wood chopping block, and can be harvested freely for [bees](/wiki/Skyrim:Bee "Skyrim:Bee"), [beehive husks](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive_Husk "Skyrim:Beehive Husk"), and [honeycomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeycomb "Skyrim:Honeycomb"). A [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") plant can be found just down the hill from the shack.

Inside the house, a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot") is behind the keg on the table. To the right of the table along the north wall is a row of three empty weapon racks. Two owned bedrolls lie on the floor to the south, with a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Father Of The Niben](/wiki/Skyrim:Father_Of_The_Niben "Skyrim:Father Of The Niben")* between them. An unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") against the east wall contains minor random loot, and beside the chest is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel. Above the chest is a weapon plaque mounted on the wall.

## Notes

- The two hunters here will often be asleep, making them excellent targets to improve your [Pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill and to feed on if you're a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism").

## Bugs

- A bottle of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom") and a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust") can be found underneath the table. The frostbite venom is in the gap between the table and the floorboard, and the glow dust is embedded into one of the table supports.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2, addresses this issue. Both items have been repositioned. They were also missing their ownership settings.

# Skyrim:Hunting and Gathering

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. | --- | |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Healing a House](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House") | | |

Elynea needs some rare ingredients

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") in the [Tel Mithryn Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Apothecary "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Apothecary").
2. Find the rare alchemy [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") she requests.
3. Return to Elynea.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After completing the quest [Healing a House](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House"), speak to [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") in the [Tel Mithryn Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Apothecary "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Apothecary") and she'll request that you bring her a particular rare alchemy [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").

The ingredient she requests can be one of the following: [briar heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart"), [daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart"), [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), [hagraven claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), or [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"). Once you have collected the ingredient, return to Elynea for your reward.

### Elynea's Dialogue

| Ingredient | Dialogue before | Dialogue after | Reward |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Daedra Heart | *Well, I could use a daedra heart. Can't grow that in my garden.* | *It's a bit dried up, but it will do. Here.* | 350 gold |
| Giant's Toe | *Hmm. I'm running out of giant toes. I'll pay extra for one.* | *A bit ripe, isn't it? Here. Take this.* | 100 gold |
| Hagraven Claw | *As a matter of fact, I need a hagraven claw. I'll pay extra if you find one.* | *Nasty bitches, aren't they? Here's your fee.* | 100 gold |
| Vampire Dust | *How about some vampire dust? Bring me some of that and I'll pay handsomely.* | *Not bad for an amateur? Take this.* | 100 gold |
| Briar Heart | *You got a briarheart? That's what I really need. Neloth keeps taking all of mine.* | *You could have cleaned it. It's still bloody.* | 100 gold |
| Void Salts | *You find some void salts and you bring them to me. I'll beat anyone else's price.* | *Hmm. Better than average quality. I'll take it.* | 200 gold |

## Notes

- If you already have the ingredient in your inventory when Elynea gives you the quest, you can immediately give it to her and complete the quest without exiting dialogue.

## Quest Stages

| 100 | ☑ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTR8 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTR8`.

# Skyrim:Hunting the Monster

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Destroy the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") target.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") |
| Location(s): | Radiant City; Radiant [Bandit Camp](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps") or [Warlock Lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs") |
| Reward: | Leveled enchanted item |
| ID: | DLC1RH04 |

Follow the trail to the vampire...

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") in [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard").
2. Learn of the [vampire's](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") whereabouts.
3. Destroy the vampire at the hideout.
4. Report back to Gunmar.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak with [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") in [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") and tell him you are ready to offer some help. He has learned of a possible monster. However, he doesn't know its exact whereabouts and will suggest you pay a visit to the [vampire's](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") last known contact to glean more information. The vampire's friend will be a notable of a random city (though not a [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl")).

Once you've found the friend, you will need to extract some information about the vampire's location by either [pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") the letter they are carrying, or pass a speech check (you'll require a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill of at least 50).

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Make this easier for you, tell me what I want to know. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: All right... Here, take this. **Failed**: Like I said. I don't know what you're talking about. | | | | **Passed**: Get the location **Failed**: Nothing |
| Perhaps some coin will jog your memory? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Well... we weren't the closest of friends... Here, take this. **Failed**: Afraid my memory can't be bought with what you've got there. | | | | **Passed**: Get the location **Failed**: Nothing |
| I'll get rough with you if I have to. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: All right, calm down... Here, take this. **Failed**: You don't scare me. **Or** You don't scare me. Let's go. **(Brawl)** | | | | **Passed**: Get the location **Failed**: Nothing |

If you're successful, you will receive a *[Letter from the Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_the_Vampire "Skyrim:Letter from the Vampire")* containing the fiend's location, which will be immediately marked on your map. It will be a random (non-quest related) [bandit camp](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps") or [warlock lair](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs") with a boss enemy.

Travel to the location and eliminate your target. You won't need to kill all other enemies to complete the quest, although in practice you often won't have much choice. Once the vampire is slain, return to Gunmar for your reward: a leveled enchanted item.

## Notes

- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).
- This quest can be repeated infinitely. After you have destroyed the target vampire, you can be sent to take care of another by taking the quest again.

## Bugs

- If the letter directs you to [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund"), and [Lu'ah](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") is already dead, there will be no boss in the dungeon and no quest marker leading you to a target.
  -  The only way to progress the quest is with the console command `setstage DLC1RH04 100`.
- An intimidation topic option during this quest may not have the brawl quest property defined, resulting in a broken call to the brawling system.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Hunting the Monster (DLC1RH04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Gunmar has sent me to <Alias=Habitation> where I am to learn the current whereabouts of the <Alias=Vampire>. I will learn this through interrogation of his last known contact <Alias=Friend>, or searching for evidence. Once its location is obtained, I am to destroy the beast in its lair. *Objective 10:* Find evidence of the vampire's whereabouts |
| 50 |  | Gunmar has sent me to <Alias=Habitation> where I have learned from <Alias=Friend> the whereabouts of the <Alias=Vampire>. I am now to journey to <Alias=Dungeon> and destroy the beast. *Objective 50:* Kill the <Alias=Vampire> at <Alias=Dungeon> |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to Gunmar |
| 255 | ☑ | Gunmar sent me to <Alias=Habitation> where I have learned from <Alias=Friend> the whereabouts of the <Alias=Vampire>. I then journeyed to <Alias=Dungeon> and destroyed the beast. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 20, 51.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RH04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RH04`.

# Skyrim:Hvitkald Peak

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

Hvitkald Peak

**Hvitkald Peak** is one of the highest points on Solstheim, west of the [Abandoned Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Lodge "Skyrim:Abandoned Lodge"). The marker for this peak does not appear on the compass until you have [climbed](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") nearly to the top.

Looking down at Bloodskal Barrow from Hvitkald Peak

Of the four marked mountain peaks on Solstheim, this is the easiest to reach. The ascent is best started from the peak's northern side, northwest of the Abandoned Lodge, at the end of the ridge just behind the exit from [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz"). Simply jump along the ridge in a southerly direction until you reach the marker.

From the top, you can see most of the Solstheim ash wastes. To the south, beyond the end of the ridge, lies the [Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall") and the [Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark") of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), while southwest is [Bloodskal Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Barrow "Skyrim:Bloodskal Barrow"). To the north, you can see Fahlbtharz, and behind that, [Mortrag Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mortrag_Peak "Skyrim:Mortrag Peak"). The Moesring Mountains extend away to the northeast, and on the eastern horizon are the steps to the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak"). On a hill to the southeast sits [Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower"), with [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)") visible to its left, and [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth") on the coast to its right. The Abandoned Lodge can be seen below you, at the foot of the mountain.

## Notes

-  The `tmm` [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command won't make the location's marker visible on the map.
- *Hvitkald* derives from the Norwegian words *hvit* meaning *white* and *kald* meaning *cold*, translating to *White Cold*.
- Hvitkald Peak also [appears](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Hvitkald_Peak "Bloodmoon:Hvitkald Peak") in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon")*.

Become the Thane of the Rift

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Befriend the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") by dealing with the Skooma trade.
2. Complete three additional miscellaneous quests in Riften.
3. Purchase [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside").
4. Return to the Jarl for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is an umbrella quest for several other quests that must be completed if you wish to become Thane of the Rift. The Jarl requires you to buy the house in town as well as completing a number of miscellaneous quests. Once this is achieved you can become Thane.

In order to receive this quest you must first aid the current jarl, [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") or [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"), by dealing with the skooma trade in Riften. This involves completing the quests [Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand"), [The Raid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid"), and [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand").

With Helping Hand and The Raid already completed, you must now complete three more [Miscellaneous Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests") specifically in Riften (for a total of five); completion of miscellaneous quests in other Rift settlements does not count, they do not have to be Favor quests like in other holds, and miscellaneous quests in Riften that were added by DLC also do not count. Note that many of the quest givers are non-essential NPCs, so their deaths would result in a loss of potential quests to complete. If they die after you assist them, they still count towards your Thane status. [Investing](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") in Rift stores does not count for this Thaneship quest either.

You must also purchase [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside"), which costs at least 5,000 gold (see [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside#Bugs "Skyrim:Honeyside")). Simply purchasing it is enough, there is no requirement to decorate, although it becomes more useful if decorated.

| [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") | [Galathil](/wiki/Skyrim:Galathil "Skyrim:Galathil") ([DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")) | **[Surgery](/wiki/Skyrim:Surgery "Skyrim:Surgery")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Change your appearance. ([DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")) *This quest does not count towards [Thane of the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift").* | - Locate the face sculptor in Riften - Talk to the face sculptor in the Ragged Flagon | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed |
| [The Scorched Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Scorched_Hammer "Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer") | [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") | **[Stoking the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoking_the_Flames "Skyrim:Stoking the Flames")**: Find 10 [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") to restore [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund")'s forge. | - Bring 10 fire salts to Balimund - Return to Balimund |  |

### Reward

After completing the necessary quests and purchasing [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside"), the journal tells you to return to the jarl. The reward, the [Blade of the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Blade of the Rift"), is a random, leveled, enchanted weapon. Despite its name, it can be nearly any weapon, including a non-bladed weapon like a Mace. There is a 50% chance that it will be one-handed and a 50% chance that it will be two-handed. You will also receive a housecarl named [Iona](/wiki/Skyrim:Iona "Skyrim:Iona"), who will be waiting for you at Honeyside.

## Notes

- Unlike every other Thane quest, the "Assist the people of <Hold>" part does not appear in the journal, and must be completed *before* the Jarl will make you the offer. A new quest "Speak to the Jarl of Riften" will appear under Miscellaneous when you have completed enough miscellaneous objectives.
- The quests which gain the favor of the jarl—[Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand"), [The Raid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid") and [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand")—are required tasks to complete before becoming named Thane of the Rift even if the Empire takes Riften, although you will be allowed to buy [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside") immediately.
- The guest bedroom in Honeyside will also be decorated at the end of this quest.

## Bugs

- "The Blade of the Rift" is never actually given as a reward: instead, you will receive a generic un-renamed enchanted weapon.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- The reward you receive is generated randomly at the beginning of the game, so will always be iron.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- Visiting Honeyside for the first time before becoming named Thane of Riften may prevent you from ever being able to be named Thane of Riften. After purchasing the house, immediately speak with the Jarl to avoid this bug.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- It is possible that the dialogue with the Jarl will not start, no matter how many people you've helped.
  -  In the console, enter `setstage FreeformRiftenThane 10`. The quest should progress normally from there.
- Sometimes the "Speak to the Jarl of Riften" step gets stuck in the miscellaneous section of the journal.
  -  In the console, enter `setstage FreeformRiftenThane 10`, and then `setobjectivecompleted FreeformRiftenThane 10 1`.
- If you have fully completed this quest and the Jarl changes during the civil war, you are unable to become thane again. **?**

## Quest Stages

| I Done Got Thaned! (FreeformRiftenThane) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Speak to the Jarl of Riften |
| 15 |  | *Objective 30:* Return to the Jarl of Riften |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Purchase Honeyside from Riften's Steward |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiftenThane stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiftenThane`.

# Skyrim:Ice Cold

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Dreamshadow](/wiki/User:Dreamshadow "User:Dreamshadow"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Chris3145](/wiki/User:Chris3145 "User:Chris3145"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

| --- | --- |
| **Find five [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth") for [Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Marise Aravel |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | Apprentice-level spell tome, five [pheasant breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften07 |

I need those teeth...

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel").
2. Find five [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth").
3. Return to Marise.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Wander around [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and you can find [Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel") and her food store at the market. She will introduce her food to you with pride: *"My food is the best in all of Skyrim; always as fresh as the day it was collected."* If you ask her for the reason to this, she will tell you she picked up a trick from a butcher in [Elinhir](/wiki/Lore:Elinhir "Lore:Elinhir"), a small town over the border in [Hammerfell](/wiki/Lore:Hammerfell "Lore:Hammerfell"). Grinding up [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth") and using it as a preservative is the key to keeping everything fresh. Then she will request you to bring her five of them to replenish her supply. You may ask her for some ideas where to find some ice wraiths. She will remind you of some potential danger and suggest you to travel to [Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent").

You may buy ice wraith teeth from [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") shops (most have a 21% chance of carrying 1-4 samples). Five samples can be found in the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment") or [Jorrvaskr Living Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr_Living_Quarters "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr Living Quarters") and four in [the White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall"). If you prefer to hunt some ice wraiths, you can easily find them in the wilderness of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). You can also find them in the following locations:

- [Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent"), recommended location, actually in [Bonechill Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonechill_Passage "Skyrim:Bonechill Passage")
- [Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave"), the previous part of the first zone
- [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"), the path to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar")
- [Tolvald's Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolvald%27s_Cave "Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave"), the previous part of the first zone
- [Weynon Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Weynon_Stones "Skyrim:Weynon Stones"), two ice wraiths will ambush you there

Once you have them, return to Marise. She will be extremely happy: *"Perfect, just perfect! These should help keep my stock fresh for quite a while."* She will reward you with an apprentice-level [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes") and five [pheasant breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast").

## Bugs

- After completing this quest once, you may receive the first quest objective in your journal again. The counter does not increase upon adding ice wraith teeth to your inventory, and the objective is stuck in your quest log permanently.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
  - Collect 10 or 15 Ice Wraith Teeth instead so that once you turn in 5, the counter maxes out at 5 again (thus successfully completing the quest).

- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften07 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften07`.

# Skyrim:Ice Mage

## Overview

**Ice Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Frost Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([fire mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage") and [storm mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of ice mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level ice mages even at high levels, but boss-level ice mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Ice Mages

A Novice Ice Mage unleashes a chilly blast

Ice mages rely on their chilling frost-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, ice mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, ice mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Cryomancers and Arch Cryomancers have the same gear as lower-level ice mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Ice Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Storms "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Storms") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Ice Mage Bosses

Apprentice Ice Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level ice mages listed above. Ice Mage Adepts, Ice Mages, Ice Wizards and Cryomancer bosses have the same inventory as the Cryomancers and Arch Cryomancers listed above, with the exception that Ice Mage Adepts and Ice Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Ice Spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Spikes "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Spikes") rather than a Staff of Ice Storms.

Ice Mage bosses are the only elemental mages that have a different outfit: they wear a different pair of generic [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006b46c "Skyrim:Clothing") and a set of [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes").

## Related Quests

### World Interactions

- **[Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic ice mages that are Nords are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means ice mages are slightly more likely to be Nords than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Ice Mage

## Overview

**Ice Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Frost Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([fire mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage") and [storm mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of ice mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level ice mages even at high levels, but boss-level ice mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Ice Mages

A Novice Ice Mage unleashes a chilly blast

Ice mages rely on their chilling frost-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, ice mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, ice mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Cryomancers and Arch Cryomancers have the same gear as lower-level ice mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Ice Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Storms "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Storms") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Ice Mage Bosses

Apprentice Ice Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level ice mages listed above. Ice Mage Adepts, Ice Mages, Ice Wizards and Cryomancer bosses have the same inventory as the Cryomancers and Arch Cryomancers listed above, with the exception that Ice Mage Adepts and Ice Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Ice Spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Spikes "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Spikes") rather than a Staff of Ice Storms.

Ice Mage bosses are the only elemental mages that have a different outfit: they wear a different pair of generic [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006b46c "Skyrim:Clothing") and a set of [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes").

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic ice mages that are Nords are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means ice mages are slightly more likely to be Nords than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Ice Mage

## Overview

**Ice Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Frost Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([fire mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage "Skyrim:Fire Mage") and [storm mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of ice mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level ice mages even at high levels, but boss-level ice mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Ice Mages

A Novice Ice Mage unleashes a chilly blast

Ice mages rely on their chilling frost-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, ice mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, ice mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Cryomancers and Arch Cryomancers have the same gear as lower-level ice mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Ice Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Storms "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Storms") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Ice Mage Bosses

Apprentice Ice Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level ice mages listed above. Ice Mage Adepts, Ice Mages, Ice Wizards and Cryomancer bosses have the same inventory as the Cryomancers and Arch Cryomancers listed above, with the exception that Ice Mage Adepts and Ice Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Ice Spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Spikes "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Spikes") rather than a Staff of Ice Storms.

Ice Mage bosses are the only elemental mages that have a different outfit: they wear a different pair of generic [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006b46c "Skyrim:Clothing") and a set of [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes").

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic ice mages that are Nords are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means ice mages are slightly more likely to be Nords than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Icewater Jetty

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Docks.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Docks.png) | Docks: Icewater Jetty ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Icewater+Jetty+%28DG%29)) | | |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC1IcewaterJetty | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| Southeast of [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") Northwest of [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep") | |

Icewater Jetty

**Icewater Jetty** is a small isolated [dock](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Places#Docks "Skyrim:Other Places") far west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and northwest of [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep").

The boat at the pier can be used to reach the nearby island to the northwest, where [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") is located. Two [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") plants, a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), a [Nordic barnacle cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), and a tree stump with [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing on it may be found in the area. Nothing else of interest is in the vicinity.

## Related Quests

- **[Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline")**: Choose your side!

## Notes

- You can hire a [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#Ferrymen "Skyrim:Transport") to take you to this location for 500 gold, from [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), Solitude, or [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). You can also travel here using the map in *[Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread_(place) "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread (place)")*[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") once this option has been unlocked.
- It is not mandatory to use the boat to access Castle Volkihar; it is possible to swim to the castle instead.

## Bugs

- The boat may overlap with the dock.
  - This appears to have been fixed with the [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition").
