# Skyrim:Ienth Farm

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

Ienth Farm

**Ienth Farm** is the home of [Garyn Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Garyn_Ienth "Skyrim:Garyn Ienth") and [Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It is in the marketplace between [Glover Mallory's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory%27s_House "Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House") to the southeast and [Alor House](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House "Skyrim:Alor House") to the northeast.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Garyn Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Garyn_Ienth "Skyrim:Garyn Ienth") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth") [Alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Alchemist") [Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Alchemy (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Alchemy (Expert)") |

### Exterior

Ienth Farm field

To the left of the entrance is where Milore Ienth generally sells her wares, with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), an open box containing two leveled [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Standard_Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a second open box containing four [torchbug thoraxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax") and a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), two unusable barrels, one of which has three more bowls of fire salts on top, and a crate all nearby. To the right of the entrance is where Garyn Ienth generally sells his own wares, with a long open box containing fourteen [ash yams](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"), a second open box containing thirteen more ash yams, an ash yam urn, an empty open chest, three crates, and an unusable barrel all nearby. The entrance has an apprentice-level lock.

The following harvestable crops and plants can be found primarily in the field north of the house, with a few plants near the southwest corner of the building beyond more unusable barrels and an empty cart:

| Crops | Plants |
| --- | --- |
| 21 Ash Yam | 10 [Scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw")  1 [Trama Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root") |

### Ienth Farm

Ienth Farm interior

The entrance leads into the upper floor of the house. Along the south wall are four unusable barrels, two of which have a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a food urn on top, respectively, two food barrels, two crates, one of which has a copy of *[The Poison Song, Book III](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_III "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book III")* on top, an open box containing four ash yams, two chairs and a table, and a bench. The table holds two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a bottle of [shein](/wiki/Skyrim:Shein "Skyrim:Shein"), a bottle of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a basket containing three ash yams. Near the west wall is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand in front of the fire, with two chairs and a small round table holding a bottle of shein, a bottle of sujamma, and a *[note](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Milore_from_Nilara "Skyrim:To Milore from Nilara")* to Milore nearby. Along the north wall is a wood pile, a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), two open boxes containing a total of ten ash yams, six sacks, five crates, two unusable barrels, a sideboard holding three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a narrow table, and a food urn. In the middle of the room, stairs lead down to the lower floor, with a bottle of shein, a wood pile with two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), three unusable barrels, one of which has copies of *[The Poison Song, Book I](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_II "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book II")* and *[Book II](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_II "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book II")* on top, and a bench around the sides of the stairs.

Ienth Farm alchemy lab

At the bottom of the stairs, to the right of a doorway are two food urns. Beyond the doorway is an area with an alchemy area to the south, a farm area to the north, and a room beyond a door ahead to the west. In the central area is an ingredient barrel with copies of *[The Poison Song, Book VI](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_VI "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book VI")* and *[The Red Year, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Year,_Vol._I "Skyrim:The Red Year, Vol. I")* on top and three unusable barrels. In the alchemy area, to the left are three ingredient barrels, two of which have an ingredient urn and a wooden bowl containing three [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") on top, respectively, and a sideboard holding three samples of [Felsaad tern feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Felsaad_Tern_Feathers "Skyrim:Felsaad Tern Feathers"), two [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a [falmer ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear"), a sample of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), a [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower, and a [potion of light feet](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Light_Feet "Skyrim:Potion of Light Feet"). In the center is an alchemy lab with a [potion of illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Potion of Illusion") on top. To the right is a set of shelves holding two [skeever tails](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), three [taproots](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), a falmer ear, two [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a [potion of resist shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Shock"), two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a [potion of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), and four sacks. Finally, to the right of the shelves is an open box containing three [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers, a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), and a sample of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot").

In the farm area are three circular ash pile plots growing a total of sixteen ash yams and ten scathecraw plants, several open boxes and baskets containing a total of thirty-two ash yams, six ash yam urns, five straw bales, and a wooden table holding two ash yams, a scathecraw sample, and a bottle of sujamma.

Ienth Farm bedroom

The room to the west is the bedroom. In the middle of the room is an owned double bed with an empty open box at its foot. Near the south wall is a chest, a small round table holding an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and three [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), a bench, a set of shelves, a chair, and another small round table holding two medium coin purses. The set of shelves holds two bottles of shein and copies of *[The Real Barenziah, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v1 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v1")* and *[v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v2 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v2")*, *[Ancestors and the Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestors_and_the_Dunmer "Skyrim:Ancestors and the Dunmer")*, and *[The True Noble's Code](/wiki/Skyrim:The_True_Noble%27s_Code "Skyrim:The True Noble's Code")*. Near the north wall are three unusable barrels, a food barrel, two chairs, and a table holding four loose coins and copies of *[The Axe Man](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Axe_Man "Skyrim:The Axe Man")* and *[Myths of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Myths_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Myths of Sheogorath")*.

## Bugs

- Several buildings in Raven Rock, including Ienth Farm, were incorrectly assigned the [music](/wiki/Skyrim:Music "Skyrim:Music") heard in [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") rather than the default Solstheim music heard in other houses.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=17929))

# Skyrim:If I had a Hammer

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Steal a legendary hammer of the gods.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatically added after purchasing the [Stendarr's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") (not visible in journal) |
| Location(s): | [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") |
| Reward: | [Stendarr's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer_(item) "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer (item)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE006\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Stendarr's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer") |

Stendarr's Hammer in the Dwemer Museum

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Gain entry to the [Dwemer Museum](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").
2. Take [Stendarr's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer_(item) "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer (item)").

## Detailed Walkthrough

**Note: This quest was originally added to your journal upon installing the [Stendarr's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). With the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), this quest no longer appears in your journal. Stendarr's Hammer can still be acquired from the Dwemer Museum.**

Go to the [Dwemer Museum](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to steal [Stendarr's Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer_(item) "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer (item)").

Note that without a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum_Key "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum Key") and [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo")'s permission, entry to the Museum is considered trespassing, and the guards inside will attempt to arrest you. In order to gain access to the museum, see the quest [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers") for more information on gaining entrance. Alternatively, you can simply pick the lock and sneak past the guards.

Picking up Stendarr's Hammer does not count as theft. However, it is exceedingly heavy (100 weight), so keep this in mind to avoid getting over-encumbered.

## Notes

- Prior to the Anniversary Edition update, you would receive this quest upon installing the Stendarr's Hammer Creation (or upon exiting [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") on a new character). With Anniversary Edition installed, there is now no notification or quest for this Creation.

## Bugs

- The quest can remain incomplete after your successful theft of the Hammer. `sqs ccBGSSSE006_Quest`  will show stage 1000 as a 0. Use `completequest ccBGSSSE006_Quest`  to get around this. **?**

## Quest Stages

| If I had a Hammer (ccBGSSSE006\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | Rumor has it that Stendarr's Hammer has been found deep under Markarth. They say it is in the Dwarven Museum there. *Objective :* Steal Stendarr's Hammer |
| 1000 | ☑ | I have successfully stolen Stendarr's Hammer from the Dwarven Museum in Markarth. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE006_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE006_Quest`.

The Iggnir River

The **Iggnir River** is a river in southern [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). For more information, see the [lore page](/wiki/Lore:Iggnir_River "Lore:Iggnir River").

# Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Fort.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Fort.png) | Military Fort: Ilinalta's Deep ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ilinalta%27s+Deep)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Lore:Ilinalta's Deep")) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 8 |
| Occupants | |
| [Necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"), [Skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star") *[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")* *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")* *[The Doors of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Doors of Oblivion")* *[Spell Tome: Soul Split](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Soul_Split "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Soul Split")*[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromantic_Grimoire "Skyrim:Necromantic Grimoire") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| IlinaltasDeep01, IlinaltasDeep02 | |
| Region | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |
| Location | |
| North of the [Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone") South-southeast of [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 1 |
| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Ilinalta's Deep

**Ilinalta's Deep** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") north of the [Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains two zones: *[Ilinalta's Deep](#Ilinalta.27s_Deep)* and *[Ilinalta's Deluge](#Ilinalta.27s_Deluge)*.

## Related Quests

- **[The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star")**: Help find and repair [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star").
- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The partially sunken fort is on the northwest shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), with only one tower and a few stretches of wall still visible. The entrance is through a trapdoor on top of part of a wall. There are several [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") on either side along the lake shore. There is also an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"), a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein"), and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") nearby to the northeast and east. A short distance east of the fort is the entrance to [South Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:South_Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:South Brittleshin Pass"). A short distance to the north is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest").

### Ilinalta's Deep

Welcome to Ilinalta's Deep

The library

When entering, you will see a shackled skeleton with a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") at its feet containing a *[Fisherman's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman%27s_Journal_(Ilinalta%27s_Deep) "Skyrim:Fisherman's Journal (Ilinalta's Deep)")*; the journal suggests the ruins are cursed and haunted. Past the shackled skeleton, you will find a larger room with a balcony ahead that is currently out of reach. The only available passage, on the left, leads to a small library. A necromancer is found sitting at a table with a companion skeleton. If he detects you, the necromancer will call for support from the next room, and a few more necromancers will join the fight. There are four bookcases around the room holding fourteen common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), five bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), and two sacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). On the table is a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a random [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), four [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment"), and a rare [human heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart"). Next to the western two bookcases, there is a table with a soul gem holder containing two more soul gem fragments. The adjoining room is a dining room, with several long wooden tables joined in a horseshoe laid with two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), two [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), and a vase with a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush growing from it. Large fireplaces are at either end of the room. Opposite the entrance is another door leading to a kitchen area guarded by a skeleton. There is a pot hanging over a fireplace to the right, and counters against the walls around the room. On the counters are two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a random [potion of waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Waterbreathing "Skyrim:Potion of Waterbreathing"), a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). There are two racks hanging from the ceiling holding a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), as well as two food barrels in the southern corner.

Continue through the halls beyond a closed wooden door to the right of the kitchen, and you will soon find yourself in a flooded room, where a skeleton and a necromancer will be ready to summon a [wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") if you are detected. There is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") along the wall on the dry side of the room, while beside the chest is a cupboard holding a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"). If you dive into the flooded part and swim down a stairway to the north, you will find a submerged bedroom, with a second chest and a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")* floating near the room's ceiling on the left as you swim into the room. Back above water, there is a door on the far side of the room heading east. The next room is guarded by a single skeleton, and contains three unowned single beds that have been jumbled together. In the northwestern corner is a large collection of kettles with a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") among them. A passage leads farther to the east.

Crafting station

At the end, the passage turns to the south and opens into a room with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"). There may be a pair of necromancers present as well; fighting the mages may alert two skeletons and a leveled necromancer (who might raise a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") to assist) from the rooms ahead. On the left is a set of shelves holding a common book, a random empty soul gem, a random potion of magicka, and a bowl. Beside the shelves is a long wooden table, where one of the necromancers was sitting. On the table is a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*, a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), three soul gem fragments, a random empty soul gem, and a random potion of magicka. There is an apprentice-locked door on the west wall, and an unlocked door opposite on the east wall. Behind the apprentice-locked door is a room with an unlocked chest, four beds, and a dresser holding three [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). Behind the unlocked door is a room with two beds and a dresser holding two potions. To the left of the apprentice-locked door is the alchemy lab. Farther along the west wall is a cupboard with an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), and a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") on a shelf. Beside this cupboard is the arcane enchanter. In the southeastern corner is a bookcase holding four common books, a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), a sprig of snowberries, a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), and a random potion of magicka. To the right of this bookcase is a passage heading south. With the [Necromantic Grimoire](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromantic_Grimoire "Skyrim:Necromantic Grimoire") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, a *[Spell Tome: Soul Split](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Soul_Split "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Soul Split")* will be on the arcane enchanter.

A necromancer

The passage turns to the west before entering a room on your right, with a small table holding a bottle of wine in front of the entrance. The room is split down the middle by water, with a bridge against the western wall. If the previous battle didn't alert the master level necromancer and two skeletons from this room, the bridge will be raised. There is a set of shelves holding two random potions of extra magicka on the right, while around to the left in the southwestern corner are two sets of shelves holding clutter, with five loose pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") between them. On the far side of the bridge is an altar holding a skeleton, a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), and a random filled soul gem. To the left is the boss chest and a chain to lower the bridge. If the bridge is raised, you will need to swim across the water to reach this chain. Under the water are two skeletons that can be looted for a few [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and an adept-locked door to the east opening to an alcove containing a set of shelves holding a random potion of healing, a random potion of magicka, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and two loose coins. There is also an unlocked chest in front of the shelves. In the northwestern corner of the room is a wooden door leading to a passage heading west before turning to the south.

At the end of the passage is a cupboard with various human bones on the shelves, while the passage staggers to the right. An apprentice-locked wooden door on the west wall opens into a storeroom, which features two barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and two sets of shelves holding a random potion of healing, a random potion of magicka, and a random potion. The passage continues south to a flight of stairs leading up. At the top, the passage turns to the west and ascends a second flight of stairs to a wooden door barred on this side. Through the door is the balcony seen in the second room at the start. To your left, a pillar has now fallen over, affording easy access to the exit. On the balcony are three empty sets of shelves and an empty long wooden table. There is a wooden door down a short passage to the north, with a stream running from beneath the door to drop into the room below as a waterfall. The door leads to *Ilinalta's Deluge*. This passage will be blocked by a large boulder if you have not yet started the quest [The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star").

### Ilinalta's Deluge

Ilinalta's Deep

Through the door is a passage that takes a few turns and descends a flight of stairs before opening into a large room. As you approach, you will hear two necromancers discussing a failed experiment and the requirement to find someone to sacrifice; they are both sitting at a table opposite where you enter the room. There is a wooden table on your right as you enter, with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top. A copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill book *[The Doors of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Doors of Oblivion")* can be found on the table where the necromancers were sitting. Additionally, the two tables at the rear of the room hold a total of eleven soul gem fragments, and each has a random soul gem—one empty and one filled—as well as a random potion of magicka on top. Between the tables is a cupboard holding a random empty soul gem and three common books. There are also two barrels of ingredients and two dressers in the room. In the northwest corner is an unlocked chest. To the west is a passage, and to the east a door opens to a storage room that contains three sets of shelves; one contains three random potions of healing, magicka, or stamina, one contains two random healing potions, and the third contains seven common books.

Malyn Varen's skeleton

The corridor to the west turns to the north and descends a flight of stairs to an unlocked door. The next hallway is patrolled by a leveled necromancer and a skeleton, and contains six empty prison cells, four of which have adept locks. The following room contains another leveled necromancer, and is shallowly flooded. The necromancer will raise a few skeletons to aid him as soon as he is alerted to your presence. The room features a raised area the necromancers have been using for sacrifices; several broken skeletons are scattered about that can be looted for gold and bone meal. Curving stairwells lead up to the left toward the next room, and down to the right deeper into the water. At the bottom of the water are two more lootable skeletons. The final room contains [Malyn Varen](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen "Skyrim:Malyn Varen")'s skeleton, [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star"), *[Malyn Varen's Grimoire](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen%27s_Grimoire "Skyrim:Malyn Varen's Grimoire")*, several lootable skeletons, and a chest, along with a ladder that leads outside to the top of the mostly intact tower in the lake.

## Bugs

- Even after starting the quest The Black Star, the path to *Ilinalta's Deluge* and Azura's Star may be blocked by a large boulder.
  - Exit and reenter the dungeon and the boulder should disappear, allowing access to the door beyond.
- The fort's entrance trapdoor may be missing, with your quest arrow pointing to solid stone.
  - A possible fix is to fast travel to another map marker (such as [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor")), then fast travel back to Ilinalta's Deep. The entrance will then be accessible.
  - Despite the trapdoor not being present, you still might be able to interact with the spot where the trapdoor would be to enter Ilinalta's Deep (i.e., where your quest arrow points). Going back out may then cause the entrance to properly appear.

# Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Daedric.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Daedric.png) | **Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Mathies](/wiki/Skyrim:Mathies "Skyrim:Mathies") or [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding") |
| Location(s): | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto") |
| Reward: | [Savior's Hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Savior%27s_Hide "Skyrim:Savior's Hide") and/or [Ring of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Ring of Hircine") (see [Multiple Rewards](#Multiple_Rewards)) |
| ID: | DA05 |

Meeting Sinding at the Grotto

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Speak to [Mathies](/wiki/Skyrim:Mathies "Skyrim:Mathies"), the father of the slain child in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").
2. Talk to [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding") in [Falkreath Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Jail "Skyrim:Falkreath Jail").
3. Hunt down the [White Stag](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Stag "Skyrim:White Stag").
4. Accept [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s challenge.
5. Face Sinding inside [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto") and make a choice.
6. Speak with Hircine.

### Falkreath

The burial of Lavinia

A plethora of battles have taken place in [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") throughout the eras, and the bloodshed has taken its toll on the small hold capital of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). The town has the questionable honor of hosting the largest graveyard in all of Skyrim, and the few resident merchants and innkeepers have named their shops or taverns in honor of the numerous deceased warriors. But while the ongoing [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") keeps its distance for the time being, Falkreath still experiences its share of death, as evidenced by a visit to the graveyard.

On your first visit (between 6 in the morning and 10 in the evening), the town priest, [Runil](/wiki/Skyrim:Runil "Skyrim:Runil"), is busy saying the last rites for little Lavinia, the only daughter of local farmers [Mathies](/wiki/Skyrim:Mathies "Skyrim:Mathies") and [Indara Caerellia](/wiki/Skyrim:Indara_Caerellia "Skyrim:Indara Caerellia"): *"The god Arkay was once like us, bound to winding mortality. But he willingly gave up this existence that we might better understand the vagaries of life and death. It is through the ebb and flow of this cosmic tide that we find renewal and, in the end, peace. May the spirit of Lavinia and all those who have left this world and its suffering know the beloved serenity of Aetherius... and may we one day rejoin them in eternity."* After the sad ceremony, the three will go their separate ways.

### Sinding

Locate the grieving father, Mathies, who can usually be found working his crops behind [Corpselight Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpselight_Farm "Skyrim:Corpselight Farm"). When asked about his tragedy he will tell you that his nine-year-old, Lavinia, was ripped apart by a laborer named [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding"), now rotting in jail for his deed. The quest will begin and Mathies' last words will be: *"What could drive a man to do something like this?"*

In Falkreath, the [jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Jail "Skyrim:Falkreath Jail") is built in the basement of [Falkreath Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Barracks "Skyrim:Falkreath Barracks"). Sinding, the alleged killer, sits in the northeastern cell waiting for his death sentence. When you get close he will approach the bars and you can ask him directly if he killed the little girl: *"Believe me, it wasn't anything I ever intended to do. I just... lost control. I tried to tell them, but none of them believe me. It's all on account of this blasted ring."*

### The Ring of Hircine

[Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding") escapes

Sinding will then show you the [Ring of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Ring of Hircine") and reveal that he is secretly a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolves "Skyrim:Werewolves") who stole the ring from the Daedric Prince of the Hunt in an attempt to control his transformations. In retaliation, Hircine cursed the ring and Sinding's plan backfired; he transformed at the worst possible time, in front of the little girl who never stood a chance. However, Sinding has a plan: *"I've been looking for a way to appease Hircine. There is a certain beast in these lands. Large, majestic. It's said that Hircine will commune with whoever slays it. I tracked it into these woods, but then had my... accident with the child. I want to beg his forgiveness. Give him back the ring. But while I'm stuck in here, the beast wanders free."* You can now offer to bring the ring to Hircine, and Sinding will gladly accept: *"Oh my. You would do this for me? Here, take it. I don't want anything to do with this wretched thing anymore. Seek out the beast. He wanders these woods. Bring him down and... well, the Lord of the Hunt should smile on you. I wish you luck, but should leave here while I still have my skin. Should our paths cross again, I will remember your kindness. Farewell."* Without the Ring of Hircine, Sinding will then transform right in front of you and claw his way to the ceiling of the cell where he disappears. When you are ready to leave, the patrolling guard may approach you and notice: *"You... you were talking to that murderous savage. And then he escaped. What are you hiding?"*

|  |
| --- |
| **NOTE**: If you are a lycanthrope, the ring will cause you to randomly transform into your beast form, which may cause a significant bounty if triggered at the wrong time. If you are not infected, the ring's only effect will be to take up your finger slot. |

### Hunting the White Stag

The [White Stag](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Stag "Skyrim:White Stag")

The [Aspect of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Aspect_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Aspect of Hircine") appears

The great beast turns out to be a unique deer named [White Stag](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Stag "Skyrim:White Stag") and can be found in an unmarked clearing east of Falkreath, usually drinking water from a small pond. If you are spotted, the stag will usually howl, then set off at a running pace up the mountain. Do your best to catch up with it, or make effective use of your long-range weapons to hit it. Once you've killed it, the [Aspect of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Aspect_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Aspect of Hircine") will emerge from the dead stag, talking to you: *"I am the spirit of the hunt, just one glimpse of the glorious stalker that your kind calls Hircine."* Naturally, as a Daedric Prince, Hircine will have a few extra tricks up his sleeve and will not simply take the ring you offer. Instead he will ask a favor: *"I may consider it. But you must first do a service for my glory. The one who stole it has fled to what he thinks is his sanctuary. Just as a bear climbs a tree to escape the hunt, but only ends up trapping himself. Seek out this rogue shifter. Tear the skin from his body, and make it an offering to me."* At this point, you can accept or decline, but it will make little difference; you are to travel to [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto"), or someone else will do it for you.

### Bloated Man's Grotto

Bloated Man's Grotto is a small cave between Falkreath and [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), normally inhabited by [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") and [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"). When you arrive during the quest, however, you will find that the Great Hunt is underway and the Bloodmoon dominates the sky. You will encounter the remains of a small hunting party, with three of the members, [Batum gra-Bar](/wiki/Skyrim:Batum_gra-Bar "Skyrim:Batum gra-Bar"), [Ma'tasarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27tasarr "Skyrim:Ma'tasarr") and [Hoddreid](/wiki/Skyrim:Hoddreid "Skyrim:Hoddreid"), already dead. A fourth member, [J'Kier](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27Kier "Skyrim:J'Kier"), is still alive, but fatally wounded. When you approach him, he will say: *"The prey is strong. Stronger than the hunters. But more will come. Bring him down, for the glories of Lord Hircine."* The wounded Khajiit will then drop dead. Loot the corpses and a locked chest behind the camp. There is also a chest in the small 'lake' where the waterfall is. After looting the chests, follow the northern path until Sinding appears on a rock above. He will be confused as to why you are there to hunt him down: *"I can't stop you if that's what you want to do. Hircine is too powerful. But if you spare me, I can be a powerful ally to you. And I would promise to never return to civilized life. I know now that I can't live among people."* He will then wait for your response, and your decision will not only affect the reward, it may also affect your achievements.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Hunted down  **Hircine's Will** If you choose to follow Hircine's will, you will have no choice but to challenge Sinding, who will respect your decision: *"So be it."* After that, he will jump down from the ledge, and you must hunt him down. At this point, several hunters will spawn in the cave, all of them under oath to the Daedric Prince, and they will all go for Sinding. Make your way up the stairs to the northeast and pass through the small ruin. There is another locked chest shortly after the 'bone alarm' doorway, on the player's right. As you make your way down in a western direction, you will stumble upon the bodies of several dead hunters, all of them too weak to kill Sinding. When you reach a small streamlet, Sinding should be finished with the hunters and will come rushing towards you. You will have no choice but to pick the fight and slay him. Activate the dead body and claim his [skin](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding%27s_Skin "Skyrim:Sinding's Skin"), and the [Aspect of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Aspect_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Aspect of Hircine"), a ghostly version of Sinding himself, will manifest before you, saying: *"You've done well, hunter."* When told that you did as commanded, he will respond: *"And found my favor. That skin will serve you well, child. Look more closely at it. My glories shall protect you from all this world's grievances. Good hunting."* He will then remove the [cursed ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Cursed_Ring_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Cursed Ring of Hircine"), and change Sinding's skin to the reward, the unique [Savior's Hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Savior%27s_Hide "Skyrim:Savior's Hide").  - Savior's Hide is the only light cuirass in the game with a resist magic enchantment, and one of only two armors. (The other armor is the [Lord's Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail")) | Hunter vs Hunter  **Help Sinding** If you choose to go against Hircine's will and spare Sinding, he will gratefully thank you and encourage you to hunt with him. Find the northeastern stairway, and join Sinding on the cliff. As you move forward, not forgetting to loot the chest on your right, you will encounter the first two hunters, [Rissing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rissing "Skyrim:Rissing") and [Tsrasuna](/wiki/Skyrim:Tsrasuna "Skyrim:Tsrasuna"), both of them hostile. Defeat them and be careful not to hit Sinding, or he will turn hostile as well. Keep moving forward and face another wave of hunters, including [Torkild the Fearsome](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild_the_Fearsome "Skyrim:Torkild the Fearsome"), [Yar gro-Gatuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Yar_gro-Gatuk "Skyrim:Yar gro-Gatuk") and [Eriana](/wiki/Skyrim:Eriana "Skyrim:Eriana"). Follow the path back to the campsite where three more hunters, [Ra'kheran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27kheran "Skyrim:Ra'kheran"), [Heratar](/wiki/Skyrim:Heratar "Skyrim:Heratar") and [Ahjisi](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahjisi "Skyrim:Ahjisi"), will attack you and Sinding. When all the hunters are dead, approach Sinding: *"Thank you for your help. I will make my home here, away from anyone I might hurt."* This will end the quest, with no reward. However, when you exit the grotto, you will encounter the [Aspect of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Aspect_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Aspect of Hircine") once again, as you failed to follow his wishes. Two options are available, and will both lead to the same conclusion: *"By bringing down my other Hunters, you turned the chase inside out. And they were no base prey. You continue to amuse and impress. Go forth, with my blessing."* He will then remove the curse from the [Ring of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Ring of Hircine") and let you keep it as a reward.  - The Ring of Hircine allows werewolves to transform an unlimited number of times per day. |

#### Multiple Rewards

|  |
| --- |
| **NOTE:** It is entirely possible to obtain both rewards, or both rings, although it could be considered cheating. Please click the show button for tips and tricks, and remember to save your game before attempting: Tips and Tricks →  **MULTIPLE REWARDS**  It is entirely possible to obtain both the Ring of Hircine as well as the Savior's Hide. In order to do so:   1. Talk to Sinding and tell him you will spare his life. 2. Help Sinding eliminate the remaining hunters. **Make sure to save your game at this point!** 3. Tell Sinding that the Hunters are dead, exit the cave and the Aspect of Hircine will appear again, granting you the Ring of Hircine. 4. Go back into the cave, give both rings to your follower/place in chest, kill Sinding, take his hide and receive the Savior's Hide from Hircine.   It has been reported that the above does not work in all cases. If you find yourself unable to skin Sinding after murdering him, reload the save from after killing the other hunters, then proceed to:   1. Tell Sinding that the Hunters are dead. 2. Kill Sinding, take his hide and receive the Savior's Hide from Hircine. 3. Exit the cave and the Aspect of Hircine will appear again, granting you the Ring of Hircine.   **BOTH RINGS**  It is possible to get the Savior's Hide and **both** Rings of Hircine, but you must have transformed to be able to do this, as you cannot unequip the ring otherwise.   1. Opt to kill the hunters rather than Sinding at the start of the quest. 2. Talk to Sinding and place the Cursed Ring of Hircine in a chest in [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto") or give it to a follower. 3. Exit the Grotto, and receive the ring from the Aspect of Hircine. 4. Go back, kill Sinding and take the skin from his body to receive the Savior's Hide. 5. Retrieve your Cursed Ring of Hircine from the chest or follower. 6. Note: If you attempt to heal Sinding he will turn hostile.   **ALTERNATE PROCEDURE**   1. Help Sinding and kill the hunters. 2. Place cursed ring in chest. 3. Go outside. Hircine will talk to you. **Don't respond. Exit the conversation and go back to the cave.** 4. Kill Sinding, skin, talk to Hircine (the one inside the Grotto) and get Savior's Hide. 5. Place Savior's Hide in chest. 6. Go outside. The other Hircine will still be there. Talk to him and get the good ring. 7. Go back to the chest inside and get the cursed ring and Savior's Hide.   **ANOTHER ALTERNATE PROCEDURE**   1. Help Sinding and kill the hunters. 2. Kill Sinding and take the skin from his body. 3. Hircine will talk to you. **Don't respond. Exit the conversation and exit the cave.** 4. Outside the grotto receive the purified ring from the other Aspect of Hircine. 5. Go back inside, turn in the skin from Sinding's body to receive the Savior's Hide.   **NOTE:**   - Depending on how you complete any of the above methods, it's possible that there will be 2 Sindings inside Bloated Man's Grotto when you return, in which case, only one of them can be skinned. |

## Notes

- This quest depicts a [Great Hunt](/wiki/Lore:Great_Hunt "Lore:Great Hunt"), a type of sporting event often associated with Hircine. A Great Hunt also occurs in [Battlespire](/wiki/Battlespire:Level_5 "Battlespire:Level 5"), [Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Hircine%27s_Hunt "Bloodmoon:Hircine's Hunt"), and [ESO](/wiki/Online:The_Great_Hunt "Online:The Great Hunt").
- This quest will completely alter Bloated Man's Grotto, but it will reset to its non-quest form one in-game month after the death of Sinding if you don't enter it during that time. It's recommended to visit Bloated Man's Grotto before doing this quest if you want to loot [Bolar's Oathblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolar%27s_Oathblade "Skyrim:Bolar's Oathblade") without killing Sinding.
  -  If you chose to save Sinding, the grotto can be reverted to its non-quest form by opening the console and entering the codes `prid 95586` and `disable`.
- Entering Bloated Man's Grotto during the quest will adjust the in-game time to 11pm, unless you enter the location between 7pm and 2am.
  - If the first case is true, you may lose your [rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping "Skyrim:Sleeping") bonus, even if you sleep right before entering the cave. If [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") is active, you may instantly incur [fatigue](/wiki/Skyrim:Fatigue "Skyrim:Fatigue") upon entering as well.
- If you exit the dialogue with Sinding after meeting him in the Grotto, or allow it to time out, it counts as having chosen to kill Sinding.
- If you save the hunters' lives when siding against Sinding, they will make their way to the grotto exit once Hircine has given you the reward and disappear from the game. If spoken to, they only have generic greetings.
- After completing the quest and leaving the Grotto, the dead hunters will disappear, along with any loot that is on them, so make sure to loot everyone before leaving.
- As you can't [enchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Effects "Skyrim:Enchanting Effects") [Resist Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic") on any armor, the [Savior's Hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Savior%27s_Hide "Skyrim:Savior's Hide") is a valuable piece of armor if you want to achieve the maximum level of magical resistance.
- It is possible to find Sinding wandering Skyrim if you should choose to let him live. He will not attack you, but cannot be interacted with in any way.
- The cursed ring gives lycanthropes a 1 in 10 chance of transforming every hour they are outdoors. Transformations won't happen indoors, nor in Bloated Man's Grotto itself (which otherwise counts as outdoors).
- Once the cursed ring auto-equips itself, you won't be able to manually unequip it. If you attempt to manually unequip it, a "You cannot unequip this item." message will appear on the top left of the screen.
- During the quest, the White Stag is referred to in your journal as the "great beast".
- If you agree to help Sinding without speaking to J'Keir beforehand, you will fail the objective to join the hunt.
- There are numerous pieces of cut content associated with this quest:
  - The hunters are numbered by group internally, but these groupings don’t correspond with how they appear in the final game.
  - [Three](/wiki/Skyrim:Mazgak "Skyrim:Mazgak") [additional](/wiki/Skyrim:Viding "Skyrim:Viding") [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Thjollod "Skyrim:Thjollod") exist, but never appear in-game.
  - The [Glenmoril witches](/wiki/Lore:Glenmoril_Wyrd "Lore:Glenmoril Wyrd") were at one point meant to also be involved in the quest. You were meant to be able to ask Sinding about them, and one of his used topics still bears the internal name `DA05SindingExplainWitchesTopic`, but his dialogue does not concern the witches and no other dialogue remnants remain. An unused [Hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") named Lucerne can still be found in the files, however.
  - In the DialogueViews, you can also find player-only topic names that no longer exist in the final game's files. `DA05GlenmorilTransformSkinBranch` and `DA05GlenmorilWarningBranch`. These topics mirror Hircine's in the final game, implying that you were originally intended to give Sinding's skin to the witches for them to transform it, rather than giving it to Hircine.
  - If you decided to kill Sinding, you were meant to lead the other hunters to him. Rissing, Ra'kheran, J'Kier, and Eriana still have specific lines for this event. Internally, they are grouped together as the first band of hunters you were meant to come across. However, in the final game they all appear separate from each other, and J'Kier suffers from a scripted death.

## Bugs

- If you acquire the [Ring of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Ring of Hircine") *and* the [Savior's Hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Savior%27s_Hide "Skyrim:Savior's Hide"), both will count towards the [Oblivion Walker](/wiki/Skyrim:Oblivion_Walker "Skyrim:Oblivion Walker") [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements"), allowing you to earn the achievement without completing one of the "required" Daedric quests. However, the "Daedric Quests Completed" statistic (in the General Stats section of your log) is only incremented once.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") addresses this issue. It now prevents you from obtaining both rewards.
- When the Cursed Ring of Hircine equips itself, it will not unequip any ring you are currently wearing, allowing you to wear two rings at once.
- It is possible for the White Stag to relocate to a location outside of the playable world, making it impossible for you to reach him and progress the quest.
  -  Use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `tcl` (make sure you have nothing targeted) to disable collision, enabling you to float towards the White Stag to kill it. Upon returning to a valid location use the same command to enable collision and resume normal gameplay.
- When leaving the jail after accepting the quest, if you don't wait for Sinding to transform and escape, he may remain there even after he is supposed to be making his way to the Grotto.
  -  It may be possible to complete the quest normally by moving him outside of the cell using `moveto player` console command and then exiting the barracks immediately.
- Casting non-offensive spells at Sinding (including healing spells) counts as striking him, therefore healing him three times will turn him hostile towards you.
- Sinding may not come to the bars when you enter the jail, making it impossible to talk to him.
  - Leaving and entering the jail a second time usually fixes this.
- If you change to beast form and then return to normal, you will be able to remove the Cursed Ring of Hircine (since transforming to a werewolf removes all items you are wearing). If you have installed [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), transforming into a Vampire Lord accomplishes the same thing.
- If you are riding a horse when the cursed ring transforms you into a werewolf, the camera will stay focused on the horse, even though you are not on it. You will need to wait to turn back into your regular form, then mount the horse and dismount it to get back to a normal camera view. This will also remove the ring.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- When Sinding attempts to escape after giving you the ring, it's possible he will fail, leaving him standing in the cell. The guards will tell you he escaped, and the hunters at Bloated Man's Grotto will still die, but returning to the jail will find Sinding still in his cage. If you then kill him in his cell, there may be two of him, one with and one without the essential flag. If this occurs, this will make the quest impossible to complete as the one you are supposed to kill will be the one with the essential flag.
- Sinding (as a werewolf) may be found back at the Falkreath Barracks, and killing him there and taking his skin will still trigger the appearance of the Aspect of Hircine, allowing you to gain the Savior's Hide long after the quest in question has been completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- After completing the quest by letting Sinding live, there may be two copies of him in the cave, both in werewolf form.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- When first encountering Sinding in Bloated Man's Grotto he may not engage you in conversation, but instead proceed to attack the hunters. However, he will be unable to properly engage them in combat and they will not be hostile to you either. You can attack and kill them, but you can't engage Sinding in conversation, making it impossible to complete the quest. **?**
  - Exit from the grotto and reenter; now the conversation should be unlocked.
- If you attack Sinding in [beast form](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy"), he may not become hostile and the option to skin his corpse may not present itself.
- If you chose to kill Sinding and skinned him in Bloated Man's Grotto, you may find his dead body also in the prison cell in Falkreath. Guards will still insinuate that you helped him escape. **?**
- If you sided with Sinding and left him alive at the end of the quest, and exit and re-enter the grotto before receiving the Ring of Hircine reward you may find the grotto completely empty, hunter's bodies removed, and with Sinding nowhere in sight. **?**
- If you get to Bloated Man's Grotto and do not find other hunters, and the quest marker leads you to a rock with nothing on it. You can use the following commands in the console to move on with the quest: 1. prid 0002abbd 2. disable 3. enable 4. moveto player
- The post quest journal entry may say *"There are stories in Falkreath of a strange vagrant who savagely killed a little girl."* **?**
- If you attempt to talk to Sinding soon after you tell him you will spare his life, he will not have any dialogue options but will instead trigger an odd scratching noise like a broken radio for a few seconds.

Bug: while siding with sinding after you kill Hunter sinding dialogue will not trigger, or there is still a missing Hunter left to kill (what to do?)

## Quest Stages

| Ill Met By Moonlight (DA05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | There are stories in Falkreath of a strange vagrant who savagely killed a little girl. *Objective 10:* Speak to Sinding |
| 20 |  | I've met Sinding, a werewolf who the Daedric Lord Hircine has punished by preventing his transformations. He's given me the ring he stole and asked me to entreat Hircine for forgiveness. *Objective 20:* Kill the great beast |
| 50 |  | I've met Sinding, a werewolf who the Daedric Lord Hircine has punished by preventing his transformations. Hircine has asked me to finish the job and gain his favor by killing Sinding. *Objective 50:* Begin the hunt |
| 55 |  | *Objective 55:* Join the hunt |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Kill Sinding |
| 61 |  | *Objective 61:* Skin Sinding |
| 65 |  | *Objective 65:* Speak with Hircine |
| 70 |  | I've met Sinding, a werewolf who the Daedric Lord Hircine has punished by preventing his transformations. I'm going to defend him against the hunters that Hircine has sent to end his life. *Objective 70:* Kill the Hunters |
| 80 |  | *Objective 80:* Talk to Sinding |
| 100 | ☑ | I met Sinding, a werewolf who the Daedric Lord Hircine had punished by preventing his transformations. I helped kill him as a service to Hircine, and have been rewarded with the Savior's Hide. |
| 105 | ☑ | I met Sinding, a werewolf who the Daedric Lord Hircine had punished by preventing his transformations. I defended him against the hunters that Hircine sent to end his life, and earned his friendship. |
| 205 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200, 210.

  Notes
- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA05`.

# Skyrim:Illusion Ritual Spell

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Bign0se](/wiki/User:Bign0se "User:Bign0se"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find some books about [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") magic to further your Illusion skills.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Drevis Neloren](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| Reward: | [Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Hysteria "Skyrim:Hysteria") spell tome, ability to purchase Master level [Illusion spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Spells "Skyrim:Illusion Spells") |
| ID: | MGRitual02 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** Level 100 [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") (see [bugs](#Bugs)) | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Level 100 [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") (see [bugs](#Bugs)) | | |

One of the four Master Illusion Texts

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Drevis Neloren](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren").
2. Find the book in [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum").
3. Find the book in [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment").
4. Find the book in [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance").
5. Find the book in [The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden").
6. Return to Drevis Neloren.

### First Steps

Once you have level 100 (see [bugs](#Bugs)) in the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") skill, travel to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). Once there, find [Drevis Neloren](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren"). Ask him if you can learn anything more about Illusion magic. He will give you a spell, [Vision of the Tenth Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Vision_of_the_Tenth_Eye "Skyrim:Vision of the Tenth Eye"), and ask you to find four [Master Illusion texts](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Illusion_Text "Skyrim:Master Illusion Text"). You can only see these books for a thirty second period each time you cast the vision spell.

### Hidden Books

1. The [first book](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Illusion_Text_(2) "Skyrim:Master Illusion Text (2)") is on a table in [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"). It is in the west on the outer ring. It appears on the same table as the book *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*.
2. The [second book](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Illusion_Text_(3) "Skyrim:Master Illusion Text (3)") can be found in the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). On the landing of the upper level, at the top of the stairs, it lies on the second step on the landing.
3. The [third book](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Illusion_Text_(1) "Skyrim:Master Illusion Text (1)") is on a barrel in the upstairs storeroom of the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance"). This is the room opposite of the room with the [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters").
4. The [last book](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Illusion_Text_(4) "Skyrim:Master Illusion Text (4)") is down in [The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden"), on a table next to the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge").

### Return to Drevis Neloren

Give all the books to [Drevis Neloren](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren") and he will give you the master-level Illusion spell tome [Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Hysteria "Skyrim:Hysteria"). You can then also buy the other three master-level tomes from him: [Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Call to Arms"), [Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmony "Skyrim:Harmony"), and [Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Mayhem "Skyrim:Mayhem").

## Bugs

- The quest only requires a skill level of 90, but Drevis's opening dialogue has a requirement of level 100, which is inconsistent with the quest and the other master level quests.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes the Master of Illusion Text books are not where they are indicated above (though they should be nearby). This is usually caused by using a spell near the location before the quest starts.
- Sometimes one of the Master of Illusion Text books will be marked as stolen in your inventory, making it impossible to give the books to Drevis and complete the quest. **?**
- The illusion book in any of the locations might not appear when casting Vision of the Tenth Eye, most commonly the books at the Atronach Forge and in the Arcanaeum.

## Quest Stages

| Illusion Ritual Spell (MGRitual02) | | |

I need to use the spell he's given me, Vision of the Tenth Eye, to find them. *Objective 10:* Bring the Four Master Illusion texts to Drevis Neloren |
| 200 | ☑ | I have found the Master Illusion Texts hidden throughout the College and delivered them to Drevis Neloren. In return, he has given me one of the Master Illusion spells. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGRitual02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGRitual02`.

# Skyrim:Imitation Amnesty

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Help get a convicted prisoner released from jail.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") |
| Reward: | Leveled jewelry, [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") is improved |
| ID: | TGTQ03 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** Five [Thieves Guild Special Jobs](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Special_Job_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in Whiterun |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | Five [Thieves Guild Special Jobs](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Special_Job_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in Whiterun | | |

The incriminating prison registry

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
2. Talk to [Olfrid Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") for the details.
3. Steal the incriminating [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Solitude "Skyrim:Letter from Solitude").
4. Forge the prison registry.
5. Tell Olfrid the job has been done.

### A Special Job

Once you have completed five Thieves Guild extra jobs in the city of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") at the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") will have a "special job" for you. Delvin explains that he has received word from [Olfrid Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born"), a wealthy [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") living in Whiterun, with a unique request. Travel to Whiterun and speak to Olfrid, who explains that "Arn", one of his old war buddies wanted for murder in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), has been arrested for drunkenness in Whiterun. In order to save his friend from the executioner's block, he wants to set Arn up with a new identity. To accomplish this he asks you to steal a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Solitude "Skyrim:Letter from Solitude") warning of Arn's true crime and then change Arn's name on the Whiterun prison registry. With these done the guards will be permanently off the trail and Arn will be given a prompt release. Olfrid warns you the job will not be easy; both items are located in [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"): the letter is in the jarl's chambers and the registry is on the steward's desk.

### Rename the Prisoner

The jarl's chambers are always accessible, but your status with the jarl determines whether you can simply walk off with the letter in his room or if you must steal it. If you do not have a standing relationship with the jarl, the guards will be on alert, so you will want to [sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") through the rooms. Closing the chamber doors before taking the letter and altering the prison ledger minimizes your chances of being caught.

### The Payoff

Olfrid is grateful that his friend will only have to spend a few days in jail for his drunkenness instead of facing an executioner's axe for murder, and gives you a random enchanted ring as a reward.

Report back to Delvin for your pay. Delvin will inform you that Olfrid has *"pledged the full support of the Battle-Born clan to the Thieves Guild"*, and that a new merchant has set up shop in the Flagon.

## Notes

- After completing this quest, three [Thief Cache](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_Cache "Skyrim:Thief Cache") barrels will appear around Whiterun.
- Although Olfrid's friend, Arn, is supposed to be in Whiterun jail for drunken behavior, he is nowhere to be found in [Dragonsreach Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach#Zone_4:_Dragonsreach_Dungeon "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"), or anywhere in the game for that matter.
  - Even the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* lists Arn as an NPC present here, and states that: *"A man named Arn is imprisoned in this location, but only after you undertake Thieves Guild City Influence Quest; Imitation Amnesty."* Implying that Arn was indeed meant to appear in-person at one point.

## Bugs

- Olfrid's essential status is not cleared after this quest like the other Thieves Guild quest NPCs.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.

In order to free him, a prisoner registry in the steward of Whiterun's quarters must be changed and a letter stolen from the Jarl's quarters in Dragonsreach. *Objective 20:* Steal the letter incriminating Arn  *Objective 30:* Forge the prison registry |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGTQ03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGTQ03`.

# Skyrim:Impatience of a Saint

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Mulsivaas](/wiki/User:Mulsivaas "User:Mulsivaas"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Collect the ten missing pages of [Saint Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub "Skyrim:Jiub")'s Opus.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Soul of Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub "Skyrim:Jiub") |
| Location(s): | [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") |
| Reward: | [Locket of Saint Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Locket_of_Saint_Jiub "Skyrim:Locket of Saint Jiub"), *[Saint Jiub's Opus](/wiki/Skyrim:Saint_Jiub%27s_Opus "Skyrim:Saint Jiub's Opus")* |
| ID: | DLC1VQSaint |
| Suggested Level: | 13 |

Jiub pacing around his campfire in the Soul Cairn

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub "Skyrim:Jiub") or start collecting pages.
2. Collect all ten pages.
3. Return to Jiub.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You may have come across a few pages floating around during your regular [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") tasks. Jiub is located in the Boneyard side of the Soul Cairn to the southeast. Talk to Jiub at any time to receive the quest, and return all ten pages to him when you have them. In return, he will give you the [Locket of Saint Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Locket_of_Saint_Jiub "Skyrim:Locket of Saint Jiub") and a complete copy of *[Saint Jiub's Opus](/wiki/Skyrim:Saint_Jiub%27s_Opus "Skyrim:Saint Jiub's Opus")*.

Staying on the entrance (staircase) side, turn right, southeast, until you reach a staircase going up into the wall. Go up the stairs and the page will be right in front of you. | [SR-quest-Impatience of a Saint 02.jpg](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Impatience_of_a_Saint_02.jpg) |

Durnehviir may be sitting on the Word Wall. The page is right on the ground next to the chest. | [SR-quest-Impatience of a Saint 03.jpg](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Impatience_of_a_Saint_03.jpg) |

Page seven and a bag of coins are on the ground at the base of the pedestal. | [SR-quest-Impatience of a Saint 08.jpg](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Impatience_of_a_Saint_08.jpg) |

It requires you to shoot a projectile (spell or arrow) through the green orbs to enter. | [SR-quest-Impatience of a Saint 09.jpg](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Impatience_of_a_Saint_09.jpg) |

Take a right (towards north) to find another Ideal Master above an even bigger building. There are several chests in this building which is a small maze, but continue until you reach the glowing symbol on the floor: a teleporting device. Stand on it to go up to the roof. The page will be next to the chest at the top of the building directly under the gem. This chest is also the one that contains the soul gem to restore you if you entered the Soul Cairn as a mortal. There are no stairs to get back down so you have to jump. | [SR-quest-Impatience of a Saint 10.jpg](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Impatience_of_a_Saint_10.jpg) |

On your right a short way there is [Morven Stroud](/wiki/Skyrim:Morven_Stroud "Skyrim:Morven Stroud") sitting. The page is on a barrel next to him. | [SR-quest-Impatience of a Saint 11.jpg](/wiki/File:SR-quest-Impatience_of_a_Saint_11.jpg) |
