Page Locations

## Notes

- It is not necessary for you to obtain this quest for the pages to appear; they can be gathered first before speaking to Jiub.

## Bugs

- The ninth page may or may not appear.
  - Try attacking near the page's spot with a weapon or spell. This should cause the page to be knocked down to the ground floor of the maze, directly beneath the archway and make it retrievable. Sometimes you cannot see it downstairs as it is glued to the ceiling.
  - Using explosive shouts or spells with a large area of effect, such as [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), can dislodge the page.
- Occasionally the sixth page will not appear in its location.
  - Leaving and reentering the Soul Cairn has been known to resolve this issue.
- If one of the inhabitants of the Soul Cairn (Boneman, Mistman, or Wrathman) is killed near any of the pages, the ashes may collect on the page, making it unobtainable.
  -  Open the console and click on the ash pile, then use `disable` to remove it.
  - Explosive spells such as a tripped ward or Firestorm will dislodge it, though multiple castings may be necessary. The page will fly off randomly, so save first in case it goes somewhere you can't find.
  - Summoning a Boneman, Mistman, or Wrathman and killing the summon by the spot the original was killed may cause the page to reappear.
- If you leave the Soul Cairn without completing this quest, your game may start to crash randomly.
  -  Return to the Soul Cairn then open the console and type `setstage DLC1VQSaint 200`. This completes the quest and resolves the crashing issues.
- Even though you've collected all ten pages, some of them may not count towards the total, leaving the quest impossible to finish. **?**
  - Open the console and type `set DLC1VQSaintCount to 10` or `setstage DLC1VQSaint 30` to fix this issue.
- The tenth page can be stuck just below the lid of the barrel and might not show up.
  - Open the console, select the barrel and type `disable`. Close the console, pick up the page then open console again and type `enable` to return the barrel back.
  - Using explosive shouts or spells with a large area of effect, such as [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), can dislodge the page.

## Quest Stages

| Impatience of a Saint (DLC1VQSaint) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | While exploring the Soul Cairn, I've come across the soul of a strange Dunmer named Jiub. He claims to be writing the second volume of his life's story but lacks the notes from his first in order to complete it. He's asked for my help in locating the pages which are likely spread across the entire Soul Cairn... quite a daunting task. *Objective 10:* Find pages from Saint Jiub's Opus (<Global=DLC1VQSaintCount>/10) |
| 30 |  | I've located all of the notes that Jiub lost when he arrived in the Soul Cairn. I should return them to him when I get the chance. *Objective 20:* Return to Jiub |
| 200 | ☑ | I've returned all of Jiub's lost notes to the poor soul. He presented me with an an *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* amulet and a pristine copy of his first volume in appreciation for my efforts. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQSaint stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQSaint`.

# Skyrim:In A Pinch

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Obtain a juvenile mudcrab for research.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") |
| Location(s): | [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") |
| Reward: | 100 Gold, [Riften Fishery Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery_Key "Skyrim:Riften Fishery Key") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Crab\_MQ1 |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [Clear-Headed](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear-Headed "Skyrim:Clear-Headed") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [Clear-Headed](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear-Headed "Skyrim:Clear-Headed") | | |

The juvenile mudcrab

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Bounty: Juvenile Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Juvenile_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Bounty: Juvenile Mudcrab")*.
2. Speak to Viriya about taking over the bounty.
3. Obtain a juvenile mudcrab for Viriya.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Mudcrab pool

The previous hire

This quest will begin while you are doing [Angler Acquaintances](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler_Acquaintances "Skyrim:Angler Acquaintances"), with you talking to [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya"):

:   *"The waiting... the insufferable waiting."*
:   **What's wrong?**
:   *"Here. I want you to have this. Don't ask. Just take it."*

She will then hand you a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Juvenile_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Bounty: Juvenile Mudcrab") for a juvenile mudcrab that she wants to study. The bounty points you in the direction of west of [Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave"). After reading the bounty, speak to Viriya:

:   **I see. You hired someone to catch a juvenile mudcrab, but they never returned.**
:   *"It would seem so."*
:   **I wouldn't mind taking over the bounty.**
:   *"Thanks. Good luck out there."*

You can either catch a juvenile mudcrab from a fishing spot with a normal rod, or you can head to the southeast of [Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument"), where there is a shallow pool. Above the pool underneath a rocky outcropping is a dead [adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer "Skyrim:Adventurer") who has a [fishing rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Fishing Rod") and a copy of the [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Juvenile_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Bounty: Juvenile Mudcrab"). The pool itself contains the remains of a colossal mudcrab, a handful of hostile mudcrabs, and a juvenile mudcrab. Either defeat or ignore the hostile mudcrabs, then find and take the juvenile mudcrab within the crook of the giant mudcrab's outstretched arm.

Once you obtain the juvenile mudcrab, head back to Riften to hand it over to Viriya:

:   **I managed to find a juvenile mudcrab for you to study. Here you go.**
:   *"Thanks. Couldn't have done that without you. I'm grateful for your efforts. Here, take this."*

Viriya will reward you with 100 gold and a key to the Riften Fishery so that you can enter at any time. The juvenile mudcrab that you give her will be found as a mudcrab called [Snippy](/wiki/Skyrim:Snippy "Skyrim:Snippy") after this quest.

## Quest Stages

She has issued a bounty for someone to obtain a juvenile mudcrab for her studies, but the last person to accept the bounty never returned. I should speak to her when I am ready to take over the bounty. *Objective 1001:* Speak to Viriya about taking over the bounty |
| 20 |  | Viriya at the Riften Fishery has been conducting research on mudcrabs in the hopes that they could be more easily bred and harvested, much like fish. She has issued a bounty for someone to obtain a juvenile mudcrab for her studies, but the last person to accept the bounty never returned. I should try fishing one up myself in the streams and lakes in the temperate parts of Skyrim. One lake in particular is known to be teeming with mudcrab, which Viriya mentioned was west of Broken Fang Cave. *Objective 0:* Obtain a juvenile mudcrab for Viriya  *Objective 20:* Speak to Viriya |
| 200 | ☑ | I turned a juvenile mudcrab over to Viriya for her research. In return, she gave me a key to the Riften Fishery so that I may enter whenever I need to. |

Notes

# Skyrim:In My Time Of Need

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Blackdove86](/w/index.php?title=User:Blackdove86&action=edit&redlink=1 "User:Blackdove86 (page does not exist)"), checked by [Panguin38](/wiki/User:Panguin38 "User:Panguin38") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Alik'r Warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") |
| Location(s): | [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den"), [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach_Dungeon "Skyrim:Dragonsreach Dungeon"), [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") |
| Reward: | 500 Gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 ([Kematu](/wiki/Skyrim:Kematu "Skyrim:Kematu")) if helping him |
| ID: | MS08 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") | | |

The [Alik'r Warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") are interrogating [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") women all over Skyrim

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get the quest from the [Alik'r Warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") in Whiterun.
2. Find [Saadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") at [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare").
3. Speak with her or report her to the Alik'r in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").
4. Kill [Kematu](/wiki/Skyrim:Kematu "Skyrim:Kematu") or lure Saadia to the stables.
5. Collect your reward from Kematu or Saadia.

### A Wanted Woman

Outside the Holds, you may come across Alik'r Warriors interrogating a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Woman "Skyrim:Redguard Woman") in the Skyrim wilderness. After [Irileth](/wiki/Skyrim:Irileth "Skyrim:Irileth") informs the jarl about the dragon attacking the [Western Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Western_Watchtower "Skyrim:Western Watchtower") during [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), you may return to Whiterun and observe an argument between Whiterun guards and Alik'r Warriors regarding their presence in the hold. Speak with the warriors to start the quest.

### Finding the Missing Woman

Go to [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare"). The Redguard is a woman named [Saadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia"). There will be a new dialogue option to tell her that some Alik'r warriors are looking for a Redguard woman. She will ask to speak to you privately. Follow her upstairs to her room, where she will draw her dagger on you, being suspicious of you - however, she quickly calms down. She explains that her real name is Iman, and that she is a noble of House Suda in Hammerfell. According to her, the Alik'r are assassins sent by the Aldmeri Dominion to deport her back to Hammerfell for an execution, as she spoke out against the Aldmeri Dominion. She asks you to help her get rid of the threat, and points you to the Dragonsreach Dungeon where one of the Alik'r warriors were captured.

There is no hard evidence provided in game by Saadia or the Alik'r that definitively supports one side. Thus, it is up to you to pass judgment and choose who to help during the quest. At this point, you can make a choice:

- Speak to the Alik'r warriors in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") and tell them of Saadia's location.
- Follow Saadia's instructions in order to help her.

There are other alternative routes (see [below](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need#Alternative_Routes "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")) that allow you to reap even greater rewards.

### Defend a Helpless Dissident...

If you decide to help Saadia, go into the dungeon of [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") and speak with an [Alik'r Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") that was captured. Talking to him reveals that he was caught sneaking into Whiterun and was captured. As a result, the other Alik'r have abandoned him, and he agrees to tell you where Kematu and the other Alik'r are hiding on the condition that you pay his fine.

Talking to him again before paying his fine will allow you to say the following - however this may cause a bug (see [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need#Bugs "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")):

:   **Let's talk about how we can help each other.**
:   *"You buy my way out of here, and I'll tell you what you want to know."*

The same dialogue will occur after you pay his fine, but there will be an option to tell him you have paid his fine. However, talking to him a second time before paying his fine may cause a bug (see [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need#Bugs "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")).

You will have to bribe the guard to set him free. Picking a guard's pocket (or murdering a guard in the jail) for the key to Whiterun's jail cells will unlock his cell - however, he will fail to register this, and insist that you bribe a guard. After paying 100 gold to a guard, the prisoner will tell you that the leader of the Alik'r is in a cave west of Whiterun called [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den").

If you have already cleared out Swindler's Den, a new dialogue option will appear when speaking with Saadia, revealing to her that you already know where the Alik'r are and allowing you to skip this part of the quest.

#### Swindler's Den

Kematu, the Alik'r leader

Upon reaching [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den"), you will find that it's full of bandits. Make your way through the network of tunnels until you reach a passage flooded with water with a waterfall at the end. When you approach the waterfall, the Alik'r leader [Kematu](/wiki/Skyrim:Kematu "Skyrim:Kematu") will say:

:   *"Alik'r, hold! You've proven your strength, warrior. Let's avoid any more bloodshed. I think you and I have some things to talk about."*

As soon as you walk through the waterfall, Kematu should initiate conversation. He explains that unlike what Saadia suggested, the Alik'r are not assassins. He claims that Saadia is wanted by the noble houses of Hammerfell for treason, for selling the city of Taneth out to the Aldmeri Dominion during the Great War. He asks you to help him bring her to justice, by leading her to the Whiterun Stables under the pretense that the Alik'r are coming for her, where he will be waiting to take her into custody.

If you still wish to help Saadia, telling Kematu at any point during the dialogue that you still intend to kill him will cause him to become hostile after telling you that he had hoped you would see reason.

Fighting the host of Alik'r warriors can be made easier by using the bear traps at the mouth of the winding path that leads into the cave where Kematu awaits. The warriors get hung up in the path, allowing the traps to be reset. Success is facilitated by focusing on your high-offense attack while retreating. Once your stamina or magic is depleted, turn and run for the traps, being careful to jump over them as you pass. It is also possible to simply exit the conversation with Kematu (or tell him that you will help lure Saadia away), sneak into the room just ahead, and snipe all the warriors with your bow.

Once the Alik'r are dead, loot Kematu's corpse for bonus gold, then return to Saadia in the Bannered Mare for your reward.

### ...Or Bring a Traitor to Justice

Saadia and Kematu at Whiterun Stables

If you decide to help the Alik'r capture Saadia, Kematu or the Redguards with whom you spoke in Rorikstead will ask you to lure her to the [stables outside of Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"). Go back and talk to Saadia in The Bannered Mare, where you can lie to her, telling her that the Alik'r are coming for her, and that a horse is waiting for her at the Whiterun Stables. Once Saadia gets to the stables, she and Kematu will have a brief exchange before Kematu will use a paralysis spell on her. Talk to him for your reward.

### Alternative Routes

While Kematu and Saadia are talking at the stables, you can still kill Kematu before he casts the spell on Saadia. This will get you the reward from Saadia and the 100 gold that Kematu is carrying, without having to fight the rest of the Alik'r. Saadia will be annoyed that you didn't warn her of what you were going to do, but she will thank you nonetheless.

Alternatively, allow Kematu to cast the spell on Saadia and collect the 500 gold reward, thus ending the quest, then kill Kematu to undo the spell on Saadia. At this point, Saadia will be hostile right away, so use a [Calm](/wiki/Skyrim:Calm "Skyrim:Calm") spell on her, then talk to her, and she will give you the 500 gold reward for killing Kematu. You can then loot Kematu's body to get 100 gold, [Hammerfell Garb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hammerfell_Garb "Skyrim:Hammerfell Garb") and [Redguard Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Boots "Skyrim:Redguard Boots"), and two [scimitars](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar"). Once the Calm spell ends, Saadia will become hostile again - this is a permanent state, so even if you leave the area, she will attack the next time you meet her. This is not a problem, as Saadia is not essential, and killing her will not give you a bounty. Looting her will give you gold and jewels. Both characters will be dead, but you will have gained 600 gold, including random jewels, scimitars, and their clothing.

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* refers to the band of Alik'r warriors as the "Alik'r Coterie".
- The Alik'r prisoner will never actually be set free, even if you pay his fine. If you retrieve the key, either by stealing it from a guard or killing one for it, unlocking the prisoner's cell does not result in anything noteworthy. He will just act as if jailed normally.
- According to the game scripts, Saadia was meant to follow until you reach Whiterun Stables but for some reason the AI package was put as escort.
- It is entirely possible to kill Saadia, as she is not essential. If you do so, her urn will show up in Whiterun's Hall of the Dead. However, if you merely turn her over to Kematu, there will be no urn in the Hall of the Dead, as the quest's script 'disables' her rather than killing her.
- Killing Kematu or his guards before starting the quest will count as murder.

## Bugs

- If you do not directly kill Kematu (i.e., Frenzy or Fury on him or the Alik'r), the quest will be stuck on "Kill or talk to Kematu". See [Quest Stages](#Quest_Stages) and skip to step 160 to progress the quest.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch") fixes this bug.
- If you kill the Alik'r warriors in the Swindler's Den, two Alik'r warriors will sometimes end up constantly appearing in Whiterun by the entrance.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- If you kill the Alik'r warriors in the Swindler's Den, encounters where Alik'r warriors harass a Redguard woman may still occur.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- After you hand Saadia to Kematu, sometimes Kematu and the Alik'r keep staying in Swindler's Den. No more conversation options are possible and the dungeon cannot be cleared.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") fixes this bug.
  -  Entering `SetLocationCleared 00018EE2 1` into the console also resets the dungeon.
- The cell where the Alik'r Warrior gets sent to cannot be unlocked.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. The door will now open with the Whiterun Jail Key like all the others.
- It is possible for NPCs who aren't guards to run the scene when talking to the Alik'r prisoner due to poor conditions on the alias check.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- Entering Swindler's Den without talking to the Alik'r Prisoner may result in the objective to talk to the prisoner never being removed from your journal.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.10, fixes this bug.
  -  Entering `setpqv MS08 DungeonFound_var 0` into the console before talking to Saadia also clears the objective correctly.
- If you speak to Kematu you'll be offered a topic that prompts "Why are you after Saadia?". This option is incorrectly assigned to him when it was instead meant to be assigned to the 2 Alik'r Warriors you initially meet if you tell them you know where to find Saadia.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, fixes this bug.
- If you choose to betray Kematu after escorting Saadia to the stables, the quest log may fail to register "Speak with Saadia" as complete no matter if you talk to her soon after defeating Kematu or once she is back to The Bannered Mare, although the game will consider the quest as finished.
- Using the alternative route mentioned above, sometimes killing Kematu after he casts the paralyze spell on Saadia will not cause her to turn hostile but will still allow you to report that the Alik'r have been taken care of, hence getting both rewards. **?**
- Sometimes if you enter conversation with the jailed Alik'r warrior a second time before speaking to the guards to pay his fine, his next dialogue option will come up early. Despite entering the new line of conversation, he will not give you the required information and your quest will not update. Paying his fine will not progress the dialogue further at this point.
  - You can reload a save to fix this, or bypass this step and go to Swindler's Den directly.

## Quest Stages

| In My Time Of Need (MS08) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | A group of men calling themselves the Alik'r are looking for a Redguard woman in Whiterun. *Objective 10:* Find the Redguard woman |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20 or 21:* Speak with Saadia *or* Inform the Alik'r of Saadia's location |
| 25 |  | The barmaid at the Bannered Mare in Whiterun is apparently a fugitive noble from Hammerfell. She claims that she is on the run from assassins sent by rival houses in her homeland and needs someone to stop them before they find her. *Objective 25 or 26:* Talk to the Alik'r Prisoner *or* Inform the Alik'r of Saadia's location |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Find a way to enter the Alik'r hideout |
| 75 |  | *Objective 75:* Enter the Alik'r hideout |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Kill Kematu |
| 101 |  | *Objective 101:* Kill Kematu or talk to him |
| 125 |  | *Objective 125:* Kill Kematu OR Convince Saadia to meet Kematu |
| 130 |  | *Objective 100:* Kill Kematu |
| 150 |  | *Objective 100:* Kill Kematu |
| 160 |  | *Objective 160:* Return to Saadia |
| 175 |  | The leader of the so-called "assassins" I've been asked to eliminate claims that Saadia betrayed her people to the Dominion and they are here to bring her to justice. I've agreed to lead her into an ambush at the Whiterun stables. *Objective 175:* Lead Saadia to the Whiterun Stables |
| 190 |  | setstage MS08 |
| 199 |  | *Objective 199:* Speak with Saadia |
| 200 | ☑ | I've helped Saadia escape the clutches of the Alik'r sent after her. With their leader defeated, she believes the rest of them will scatter, affording her some much-needed safety for now. |
| 201 | ☑ | After making arrangements with Kematu, I've delivered Saadia to him. He assures me that she will be taken back to Hammerfell alive, though after that her fate is no longer in his hands. |
| 300 | ☒ |  |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 130:* Kill Kematu |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS08 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS08`.

# Skyrim:In the Shadows

## Overview

|  |

| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") or [Brill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brill "Skyrim:Brill") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the [Steward's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward%27s_Note "Skyrim:Steward's Note").
2. Take the ledger copy at Arcadia's Cauldron.
3. Read the Business Ledger Copy.
4. Investigate the Hall of the Dead.
5. Check the stables.
6. Investigate the Silent Moons Camp.
7. Find the Assassin on the upper floor of Dragonsreach when the Jarl is unoccupied.
8. Retrieve the Bow of Shadows.
9. Speak to the Jarl's Steward.

### An Assassination Plot

Talk to the current [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") of Whiterun (typically either [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") or [Brill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brill "Skyrim:Brill")) and ask if he has anything for you. He will hand you a note, explaining that he is concerned of an assassination plot on [the Jarl of Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarls "Skyrim:Jarls") from an anonymous informer. He dare not tell it to you out loud due to the Jarl already having plenty on his plate, as well as the fact that he is unsure of its credibility.

The steward would like you to visit [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron") and look through their business ledger to spot any suspicious purchases; to this end he has asked [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia") to leave you a copy to peruse.

### Suspicious Purchases

Head to Arcadia's Cauldron and you will find the business ledger on the counter. Unlike [the typical business ledgers](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Numbers_Job "Skyrim:The Numbers Job"), this one you can pick up; do so and look through it to find that two people - a Priest of Arkay and a Nord Stable Boy - have made purchases of poisons. Time to investigate and look at their motives for doing so.

#### The Hall of the Dead

Enter the Hall of the Dead and then the Whiterun Catacombs; note that if you have not entered this location before there will be hostile [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") in this area - either kill or avoid them. Once you enter, descend down the flight of stairs to your left and you will find a dead skeever, a block of cheese, the poison in question and a note, explaining that the poison had been applied to the cheese in an attempt to rid the place of the skeever infestation.

#### Whiterun Stables

Exit Whiterun proper and down the path to the stables, where you will find a dead Nord behind a haystack of the leftmost stall. Beside him will be a [lunar steel weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Items#Lunar_Weapons "Skyrim:Leveled Items"). Loot the Nord and find upon him a note as well as a [spell tome of Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)"); like before, read the note and find that the Nord has been posing as a stable boy. The note also states that he was supposed to meet a Dark Elf at this location instead of at [Silent Moons Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Moons_Camp "Skyrim:Silent Moons Camp") and the spell tome was to help the Nord in locating him as the Dark Elf snuck up on him the last time, though he was apparently unable to get the spell working.

### Off to Silent Moons Camp

Now that you have your next destination, make your way to Silent Moons Camp. Your objective is at the very back, so if you are so inclined you may opt to go around and hop over the wall, but whichever way you choose, a journal of an assassin will be lying on a table just outside the room containing the [Lunar Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge#Lunar_Forge "Skyrim:Forge"). Again, pick it up and read it, finding largely ramblings but an important detail: the author of this book shall be waiting on the second floor of Dragonsreach, waiting for an opportune time to strike and kill the Jarl.

### Back Where We Started

Return to Dragonsreach and head up the stairs on the right of the main hall to the second floor, then turn around and make your way out onto the balcony. The area looks clear, but once you reach the end you will find the Dark Elf assassin in question, who had been hiding under a cloak of [invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(effect) "Skyrim:Invisibility (effect)"); at this point he will become hostile and attack you. (You may also cast Detect Life to locate him if you have learned it from the spell tome you should have obtained earlier, however as he will cease to be invisible once you get close it is not necessary.) He is quite decently armed and can pose a fatal threat if you're of lower level, but luckily you have allies who will help if you lure him downstairs.

*Note:* Rather uniquely, the assassin is marked as [protected](/wiki/Skyrim:Protected_NPCs "Skyrim:Protected NPCs"), which means he cannot be killed by other NPCs and the killing blow must be dealt by the player.

The assassin will not appear if the Jarl is occupied, and will not appear if you haven't started the quest [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"). The Jarl is considered occupied when the following quest stages are active:

- [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") - Stage 10: When Jarl Balgruuf is showing you to [Farengar](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire").
- [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") - Stages 10, 12, 13, 15, 20, 110, 120, 130, 150: During the scenes inside Dragonsreach at the beginning of the quest and after the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") summon you to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar").
- [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") - Stages 25, 27 - When persuading the Jarl about to trap [Odahviing](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") in Dragonsreach.
- At any point during [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun"), [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude"), or [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm").

Once the assassin is dead, loot his corpse and find the Bow of Shadows. Speak to the steward again and gain a monetary reward.

### Reward

| Level | Gold |
| --- | --- |
| 1-9 | 500 |
| 10-19 | 750 |
| 20-29 | 1000 |
| 30-39 | 1250 |
| 40+ | 1500 |

## Notes

- The foray into Silent Moons Camp is a chance to pick up the six Lunar Iron/Steel weapon variants.
- The deceased Nord in the Stable carries the Detect Life spell tome which is a good chance to pick it up early on. Detect Life can help level Alteration quickly and is otherwise hard to obtain.

## Bugs

- If you finish [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"), [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen"), [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun"), [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude") or [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") and the Jarl is not occupied, the assassin does not appear.
  -  This can be resolved using console commands to manually advance the quest. Using: `prid FExxx82F, kill, setstage ccBGSSSE038_Quest 80, openactorcontainer 1` This will kill the Assassin, update the quest so that he is dead, and allow the player to loot his inventory to take the Bow, which advances the quest once more so that you can talk to the Steward and collect the reward, ending the quest. You can use `player.additem FExxx807 1`  to get the Bow of Shadows
  -  Alternatively, using the console command `prid FExxx82f` and then `enable` or `placeatme FExxx808` may allow the assassin to spawn in correctly, letting the player kill them normally and finish the quest as intended.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.

It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE038_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Inaccessible Cells

## Overview

This is a list of **Test Cells** and **Unused Cells** in Skyrim's data. They may be accessed by typing `coc [editor ID]` into the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"). Multiple cells may share a name, but not an editor ID. For some cells, it may be necessary to toggle clipping (console command `tcl`) to reach certain areas. For information on unused content in general, please see the [related page](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_Content "Skyrim:Unused Content").

## Holding Cells

Holding cells exist in order to hold items until they are needed by a quest or something else.

### Bard Holding Cell

DLC2HoldingCellBard

:   *Editor ID: DLC2HoldingCellBard*

This interior cell, added by Dragonborn, contains a DLC2dunInstrumentNPC, the spectral drum summoned by the power [Bardic Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Knowledge "Skyrim:Bardic Knowledge").

### DLC1LD Holding Cell

DLC1LD Holding Cell

:   *Editor ID: DLC1LDUtilityCell*

This interior cell, added by [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), has stone walls of Dwemer architecture. On one end is a table with the [Aetherial Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Crown "Skyrim:Aetherial Crown"), [Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Staff "Skyrim:Aetherial Staff"), and [Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Shield "Skyrim:Aetherial Shield"), plus an [Aetherium Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherium_Crest "Skyrim:Aetherium Crest"), with a duplicate Crest that cannot be picked up by you.

### DLC1 Item Holding Cell

DLC1 Item Holding Cell

:   *Editor ID: DLC1VQHoldingCell*

This interior cell, added by Dawnguard, has a wooden table in the middle. On top of the table is an [Initiate's Ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer") and four books: [Unknown Book, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._I "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. I") through Vol. IV. It is impossible to take these books; they play the correct audio yet cannot be taken. To the left of the table is a safe which holds some Dawnguard-specific books, the list of which can include Elder Scrolls.

### DLC1LD Quest Holding Cell

DLC1LD Quest Holding Cell

:   *Editor ID: DLC1TestCellRJ*

This interior cell, added by Dawnguard, is similar to Soul Cairn architecture. It contains a number of small, ruined towers, with some scattered human bones, piles of human bones, and a few dead trees. Far beneath this is a tiny cave room.

### Do Not Delete - Not A Test Cell

ThievesGuildHoldingCell

:   *Editor ID: ThievesGuildHoldingCell*

This interior cell has a number of wooden tables in it. In the southeastern corner is a naked woman with [Vaermina](/wiki/Skyrim:Vaermina "Skyrim:Vaermina")'s name and voice, but she is disabled and may not appear. In the northwestern corner are three chests: [Zaynabi](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaynabi "Skyrim:Zaynabi"), [Atahbah](/wiki/Skyrim:Atahbah "Skyrim:Atahbah"), and [Ma'jhad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27jhad "Skyrim:Ma'jhad")'s [Merchant Chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"); all three are Thieves Guild fences. On the table in the northeastern corner are a keg of Black-Briar Mead, the *[Goldenglow Bill of Sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Bill_of_Sale_(Gulum-Ei) "Skyrim:Goldenglow Bill of Sale (Gulum-Ei)")*, *[Gallus's Encoded Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal")*, and *[Gulum-Ei's Confession](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei%27s_Confession "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei's Confession")*. To the right of this table is a safe containing gold, jewelry, gems, special loot, and ingots.

In the middle of the room is a set of five tables pushed together. To the left of these tables is an unsupported door. The southern two tables hold twelve [Stones of Barenziah](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") each, neatly aligned in rows of six. On the middle of the three northern tables is the [Skull of Corruption](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull_of_Corruption "Skyrim:Skull of Corruption"). The easternmost table has three satchels on it: [Verner's Satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Verner%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Verner's Satchel"), [Sylgja's Satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Sylgja's Satchel"), and a [Satchel of Moon Sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel_of_Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Satchel of Moon Sugar"). [Klimmek's Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek%27s_Supplies "Skyrim:Klimmek's Supplies"), a sack, lies on the table as well. Also on the table are [Sinderion's Field Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Journal "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Journal"), a bottle of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), a bottle of [Honningbrew Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"), and [Firebrand Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebrand_Wine "Skyrim:Firebrand Wine").

Two more occupied tables are just north of Vaermina. The western one has *[The Nightingales Vol. 1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Nightingales_Vol._1 "Skyrim:The Nightingales Vol. 1")*, *[The Nightingales Vol. 2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Nightingales_Vol._2 "Skyrim:The Nightingales Vol. 2")*, *[Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales:_Fact_or_Fiction%3F "Skyrim:Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?")*, *[Shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(book) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (book)")*, *[Promissory Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Promissory_Note "Skyrim:Promissory Note")*, and *[Goldenglow Bill of Sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Bill_of_Sale_(safe) "Skyrim:Goldenglow Bill of Sale (safe)")*. The eastern one has [Chillrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillrend "Skyrim:Chillrend") and all items involved in the quest [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"). There is another table to the south, but this has nothing.

### Dremora Holding Cell

DLC2DremoraShop

:   *Editor ID: DLC2DremoraShop*

This interior cell, added by [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), contains the [Dremora Butler](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Butler "Skyrim:Dremora Butler"), the [Dremora Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Merchant "Skyrim:Dremora Merchant") and his merchant chest.

### holding cell

:   *Editor ID: DLC1NPCHome*

This interior cell, added by Dawnguard, is modeled like a Nordic barrow. It is a single square room with two very short hallways with dead ends.

:   *Editor ID: Elsweyr*

This interior cell has stone walls. It holds [M'aiq the Liar](/wiki/Skyrim:M%27aiq_the_Liar "Skyrim:M'aiq the Liar"), but he is disabled and does not appear.

### Marker Storage Unit

aaaMarkers

:   *Editor ID: aaaMarkers*

This interior cell has no ground. It holds a number of quest-specific markers (including a [fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity) "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") marker with the Fishing Creation) and an Ancient Dragon.

### Raven Rock Holding Cell

DLC2RRHoldingCell

:   *Editor ID: DLC2RRHoldingCell*

This interior cell, added by Dragonborn, holds an unlocked safe containing [Letter to Imperial City](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_Imperial_City "Skyrim:Letter to Imperial City")

### [Unnamed Cell]

:   *Editor ID: BYOHHouseUtilityCell*

This interior cell, added by [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), has no ground. It holds a number of chests, an NPC called [Fish Hatchery](/wiki/Skyrim:Fish_Hatchery "Skyrim:Fish Hatchery"), and several NPCs called Planter.

DLC2aaaMarkers

:   *Editor ID: DLC2aaaMarkers*

This interior cell, added by [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), has a tiny platform, a black book effect, and a number of markers relating to the Dragonborn add-on.

### Unowned Cell

UnownedCell

:   *Editor ID: UnownedCell*

This interior cell holds an unowned Chest, which contains an [Amulet of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Mara "Skyrim:Amulet of Mara"). This cell is also used in a Creation Kit tutorial by Bethesda: "Creation Kit Tutorial Series - Episode 1: Introduction to the Kit"

### Warehouse Bookshelves

WEMerchantChests

:   *Editor ID: WEMerchantChests*

This interior cell holds the [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest") for the two [Peddlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Peddler "Skyrim:Peddler"); it is empty.

## Test Cells

Test cells are used to test how things look, work, or interact with each other.

### CWSiegeTestWorld

This worldspace contains a number of cells, just as Tamriel does. To reach these cells, type `cow CWSiegeTestWorld x,y` into the console. Typing `cow CWSiegeTestWorld 0,-3` will get you into the cell with editor ID *SiegeStart*; the rest are named *Wilderness*, just like many of Tamriel's cells. The world consists of 26 cells, which are highlighted in green.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Y | 1 |  |  |  |  |  |
| 0 |  |  |  |  |  |
| -1 |  |  |  |  |  |
| -2 |  |  |  |  |  |
| -3 |  |  |  |  |  |
| -4 |  |  |  |  |  |
| -5 |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | | -2 | -1 | 0 | 1 | 2 |
| X | | | | |

The worldspace consists of a large, walled-in area with multiple short walls inside. There is nothing of interest there.

### CWTestHold

This worldspace contains a number of cells, just as Tamriel does. To reach these cells, type `cow CWTestHold x,y` into the console. There is a large number of Wilderness cells, which are all empty; the others are mostly but not completely bare. To enter cell with editor ID *TestCWHoldStart*, type `cow CWTestHold 0,0`.

| Cells | |
| --- | --- |
| Editor ID | Coordinates |
| TestCWBarleyDarkFarm | -1, 1 |
| TestCWBattleBornFarm | 2, 1 |
| TestCWCampImperial | -1, -1 |
| TestCWCampSons | 1, -1 |
| TestCWChillfurrowFarm | 2, 0 |
| TestCWFortBlackmoor | -1, 0 |
| TestCWHoldStart | 0, 0 |
| TestCWPatrolsImperial | -1, -2 |
| TestCWPatrolsSons | 1, -2 |
| TestCWPelagiaFarm | 2, -1 |
| TestCWRiverwood | 1, 1 |
| TestCWRorikstead | 0, 1 |
| TestCWWhiterunNoLOCATIONDATA | 3, 0 |
| TestCWxxx | 4, 0 |

The buildings in this worldspace are all far apart and all appear the same, with the exception of a grain mill. To the east is a set of short, stacked walls, creating an odd appearance. There are areas of this worldspace in which not even footsteps make a sound.

- 

  TestCWHoldStart
- 

  TestCWWhiterunNoLOCATIONDATA

### Editor Smoke Test Cell

QASmoke

:   *Editor ID: QASmoke*

A dungeon atmosphere room containing several [crafting tools](/wiki/Skyrim:Activities "Skyrim:Activities") and [containers](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers "Skyrim:Containers") with a collection of all items in the game.

The tools are:

:   2 Alchemy Lab, 2 Arcane Enchanter, Blacksmith Forge, Anvil, Grindstone, Smelter, Tanning rack, Cooking Spit, Pot and Workbench.

The containers storing the appropriate items are labeled:

:   "All [Ammo](/wiki/Skyrim:Ammunition "Skyrim:Ammunition")", "All [Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books")", "All [Clothing and Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing")", "All [Enchanted Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel")", "All [Enchanted Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")", "All [Ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients")", "All [Keys](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys "Skyrim:Keys")", "All [Misc Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items")", "All [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions")", "All [Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls")", "All [Skill Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books")", "All [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems")", "All [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes")", "All [Staves](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves")", "All [Standard Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor")", "All [Standard Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons")"

Furthermore, you can find a table with three wooden ladles lying on it near the end of the main corridor.

With the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on, an extra hall with two containers labeled "All [Dawnguard Misc or Other Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Items#Other_Items "Skyrim:Dawnguard Items")" and "All [Dawnguard Weapons and Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Items#Armor "Skyrim:Dawnguard Items")" is added. You can go through the end of the main corridor to get there.

[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") expands two new cells in the north.

The first cell has several chests for Dragonborn specific items. From left to right, they are labeled:

:   "All Dragonborn [Keys](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys "Skyrim:Keys")", "All Dragonborn [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes")", "All Dragonborn [Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls")", "All Dragonborn [Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books")", "All [Dragonborn Misc Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items")", "All Dragonborn [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions")", "All Dragonborn [Ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients")", "All Dragonborn [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear "Skyrim:Specialty Gear")", "All Dragonborn [Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons")", "All Dragonborn [Ammo](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons#Arrows "Skyrim:Weapons")"

You can also find a small deep pool (presumably to test [water walking](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterwalking "Skyrim:Waterwalking")) and four practice dummies. There are two activators near the door to the second cell. Activating the left button will teach you all words for [shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") added in Dragonborn. Activating the right button will teach all [spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells") added in Dragonborn. Both buttons can be activated only once.

The second cell contains 7 buttons and a barrier with an unlocked door. By activating a button, you can spawn a creature behind the barrier. You can activate each button many times and spawn multiple creatures at the same time. Once a button is activated, you must choose to spawn a creature to quit the interface. In most cases, they will fight with each other and turn hostile to you. Be careful, some of them may open the door and attack you. Detailed information about each button (from left to right) can be found below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

[†](#note_Not_found)Only appear in test cell.

[‡](#note_Bug)Probably a bug. A *bristleback* is a boar, while a *fire wyrm* is a spectral dragon.

- All spawned creatures have common loot.
- Spawned creatures may get out of the cage as long as their sizes allow them to cross the door.
- Spawned frost giant won't drop [Paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Portal "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale").
- Spawned fire wyrm won't turn hostile to you.

### FXLightWorldSpace

This worldspace contains a large number of cells, just as Tamriel does. To reach these cells, type `cow FXLightWorldSpace x,y` into the console. All of these cells are empty and are nothing but land. To enter one cell of this worldspace, type `cow FXLightWorldSpace 0,0`.

### Its baaaaaack

:   *Editor ID: testFalmer*

This interior cell, added by Dawnguard, is set up like a stone fortress. Behind the entrance is empty space. There are Ancestor Moths in the middle of the main room, with three locations on the ground where they can land. There is nothing of interest up the stairs. A leveled melee bandit stands next to the doorway, through which there is a small room. Embers float next to a broken part of a wall, which leads to a dirt tunnel with wooden support beams. The tunnel ends in nothingness.

:   *Editor ID: testGiant*

This interior cell, added by Dawnguard, is set up like a stone fortress. Behind the entrance is empty space. In the middle of the main room is a weak test vortex with a number of items in it—four Iron Daggers, two Hide Shields, two Deathbell flowers, one [Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Greatsword_of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno"), and four bloody human leg bones. In one corner of the room is a test Storm Atronach (level 30), but it is disabled and does not appear. There is nothing of interest up the stairs. Through the doorway, there is a small room with floating embers next to a broken part of the wall, which leads to a dirt tunnel with wooden support beams. The tunnel ends in nothingness.

The vortex and atronach both have "test" and "Phil" in their editor IDs, showing that they are specifically test objects and possibly made or used by a guy named Phil.

### Magic Visuals Test Hall

An overview of XTestGrantInt

:   *Editor ID: XTestGrantInt*

This interior cell is huge, with stone walls. Throughout it, there is the sound of bells. The southernmost room, in the southeast, tests mist. Heading through a short hallway north, the next room has more mist and a jet of steam. The next room, to the west, contains no mist but a test HDR box that appears to have multiple color bars on it of varying intensities. Heading through a misted hallway to the north ends in a room with a test white light, two unusable doors (one unsupported), a barrel of food, a few ice spikes on the floor, a static light spell in the west, and a Circle of Protection near the middle.

There are two doorways to the north of this. The hall through the left one has gas traps throughout, as does the resulting room, which is the center of a set of three. It contains [Hide Armor of Minor Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor_of_Minor_Health "Skyrim:Hide Armor of Minor Health"). The cell to the left has test violet light and static test lightning; in its southwestern corner are two food barrels, some ice spikes on the ground, some fire effects, and test blue lighting. The third of the rooms has test particle lighting, test blue lighting, and the light of a magical fire barrier. Its southern door leads to an unconnected room in the same cell that looks like an inn's common room. In the middle is test bounce lighting and to the west is test candle lighting. The campfire light is a test as well. Also in the room are an Iron Mace and Iron War Axe of Embers.

Heading back to the three side-by-side rooms, each of them has a door heading north to three side-by-side hallways. The easternmost of these is a dead end and does not connect to the other two. It contains another test HDR box, two downwards frost rune traps, one sideways fire rune trap, and one downwards lighting rune trap. It has the light from a magic barrier on top of fire effects.

In the middle hallway, which is misted, there are some soul gems sticking out of rocks near a static Sphere Centurion. There is oil on the ground. There is a test orange light near the ground (this one including the name "Cory" in its ID), and there is a test ray of sunlight near the end of the hall. The left hall has test candlelight and another static Centurion, which is holding a candle in its left hand, with oil on the ground but no fog. There is nothing beyond the end door of this hall.

Through the doorway at the end of the middle hall is the northernmost room. There is a house on the left side with no door or entrance. There is an oil slick on one side of the house and another near the entrance the room. There is a fire pillar with some magic fire light effect next to it. Another copy of this light is about halfway between an oil slick and the fire pillar.
